<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>I really don't think they should let the <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">other sort</a> in, do you? They're just not the same, they've never been brought up to know <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">our</a> ways. Some of them have never even heard of Hogwarts until they get the letter, I imagine. I think they should keep it in <a href="/wiki/Sacred_Twenty-Eight" title="Sacred Twenty-Eight">the old wizarding families</a>.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco showing his <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">prejudice</a> at a young age<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><b>Draco Lucius</b><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> <b>Malfoy</b> (b. <a href="/wiki/5_June" title="5 June">5 June</a> <a href="/wiki/1980" title="1980">1980</a>) was a <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> and the only son of <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius</a> and <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> <span class="template-c">(née <a href="/wiki/House_of_Black" title="House of Black">Black</a>)</span>. The son of a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>, Draco was raised to strongly believe in the importance of <a href="/wiki/Blood_status" title="Blood status">blood purity</a>. He attended <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> from <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>-<a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a> and was sorted into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a>. During his years at Hogwarts, he became friends with <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a>, and other fellow Slytherins, but he quickly developed a rivalry with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>.
</p><p>He was made a <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> of his house and was a member of the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a> during his fifth year, at the end of which his father was imprisoned in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> following the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>. <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> charged Draco with making up for Lucius's failure, and he became a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> at age sixteen but was quickly disillusioned with the lifestyle. Draco was unable to complete his task of murdering <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, which was later taken over by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, and only performed his other duties fearfully and reluctantly. He and his family defected hours before the end of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, fearing for their lives.              
</p><p>By <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, Draco had married <a href="/wiki/Astoria_Malfoy" title="Astoria Malfoy">Astoria Greengrass</a> and had one child, <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Hyperion Malfoy</a>. 
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Early_life_(1980-1991)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_.281980-1991.29">Early life <span class="template-c">(1980-1991)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life (1980-1991)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early life (1980-1991)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Growing_up_in_Malfoy_Manor">Growing up in Malfoy Manor</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Growing up in Malfoy Manor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Growing up in Malfoy Manor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Draco_Black_Malfoy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150729181422" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="198" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco Black Malfoy.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Black_Malfoy.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Draco_Black_Malfoy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150729181422" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Draco_Black_Malfoy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150729181422" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Draco_Black_Malfoy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150729181422" decoding="async" width="180" height="198" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco Black Malfoy.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Black_Malfoy.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Draco_Black_Malfoy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150729181422" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_Black_Malfoy.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco on the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Black" title="House of Black">Black Family Tree</a> tapestry</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Draco Lucius Malfoy was born on <a href="/wiki/5_June" title="5 June">5 June</a> <a href="/wiki/1980" title="1980">1980</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius</a> and <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> (née <a href="/wiki/House_of_Black" title="House of Black">Black</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> who were both born into old, wealthy <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> families. Both the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoys</a>' and the Blacks had traditionally been in <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a> for centuries and strongly disapproved of any relatives who did not follow in this tradition, such as <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a><sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Draco was raised in an atmosphere of regret that the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> had not succeeded in taking command of the wizarding community, although he was prudently reminded that such sentiments ought not to be expressed outside the small circle of the family and their close friends 'or Daddy might get into trouble'. The <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoys</a>' were very proud of their <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">Pure-blood</a> and social status; until <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, they were able to maintain a respectable public image while being allied with <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>. Lucius was a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> who avoided imprisonment in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> following the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a> by claiming that he had been under the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a>, while <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa</a> merely agreed with the ideology of <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">pure-blood supremacy</a>. 
</p><p>The Malfoys spoiled their son, giving him the best of everything as far as material possessions go. The only two hand-me-down things Draco ever received were the old family prejudice against <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a>, <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a>, <a href="/wiki/Half-breed" title="Half-breed">half-breeds</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Blood_traitor" title="Blood traitor">blood traitors</a> — in short, prejudice against anyone who was not a pure-blood wizardkind, or anyone who supports these types of people — and the Malfoy family's waste collection of powerful dark artefacts harking back to the family history.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preparing_for_Hogwarts">Preparing for Hogwarts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Preparing for Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Preparing for Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/Albus_Dumbledore%2C_Draco_Malfoy_and_Lucius_Malfoy_from_Harry_Potter_Hogwarts_Mystery.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200609052836" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore, Draco Malfoy and Lucius Malfoy from Harry Potter Hogwarts Mystery.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore,_Draco_Malfoy_and_Lucius_Malfoy_from_Harry_Potter_Hogwarts_Mystery.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/Albus_Dumbledore%2C_Draco_Malfoy_and_Lucius_Malfoy_from_Harry_Potter_Hogwarts_Mystery.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200609052836" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/Albus_Dumbledore%2C_Draco_Malfoy_and_Lucius_Malfoy_from_Harry_Potter_Hogwarts_Mystery.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200609052836" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/Albus_Dumbledore%2C_Draco_Malfoy_and_Lucius_Malfoy_from_Harry_Potter_Hogwarts_Mystery.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200609052836" decoding="async" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore, Draco Malfoy and Lucius Malfoy from Harry Potter Hogwarts Mystery.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore,_Draco_Malfoy_and_Lucius_Malfoy_from_Harry_Potter_Hogwarts_Mystery.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f2/Albus_Dumbledore%2C_Draco_Malfoy_and_Lucius_Malfoy_from_Harry_Potter_Hogwarts_Mystery.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200609052836" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore,_Draco_Malfoy_and_Lucius_Malfoy_from_Harry_Potter_Hogwarts_Mystery.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco with his father and Dumbledore at Hogwarts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In childhood, Draco associated mainly with the pure-blood children of his father's ex-<a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> cronies and therefore arrived at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> with <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy%27s_gang" title="Draco Malfoy&#39;s gang">a small gang of friends</a> already made, including <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Nott" title="Theodore Nott">Theodore Nott</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a>. He visited the school himself when Lucius came to inspect, and his father entrusted <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> and <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a> to babysit him, a decision which did not rub off well with any of the three. Lucius had requested the two in particular, as Jacob's sibling was ostensibly the best student in their year, whilst Merula was the daughter of two of Lucius' former Death Eater colleagues and thus considered the "right" type of person for Draco to associate with. Draco did not endear himself to either student, however, particularly with his snobbish and disdainful attitude towards them and open displays of prejudice.
</p><p>During the visit, Draco stole his father's wand, as he was too young to have his own and wanted to perform magic after seeing Merula perform the <a href="/wiki/Jelly-Legs_Curse" title="Jelly-Legs Curse">Jelly-Legs Curse</a> on Jacob's sibling. Lucius initially blamed the theft on their <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elf</a> <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a>, as the perpetrator knew he kept <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy%27s_wand" title="Lucius Malfoy&#39;s wand">his wand</a> inside his <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy%27s_walking_stick" title="Lucius Malfoy&#39;s walking stick">walking stick</a>, which wasn't common knowledge. Jacob's sibling investigated, and returned the wand to Lucius.<sup id="cite_ref-HM_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When the time came for Draco to attend school in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, his <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">father</a> wanted him to attend <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang Institute</a>, a school in Northern <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> that taught the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> and did not admit <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a>. However, his <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">mother</a> did not like the idea of Draco going to school far away, thus they sent him to Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Draco went to <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> to shop for school supplies in 1991, he met <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> in <a href="/wiki/Madam_Malkin%27s_Robes_for_All_Occasions" title="Madam Malkin&#39;s Robes for All Occasions">Madam Malkin's Robes for All Occasions</a>, without knowing who he was. He made a rather intolerant speech about <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, but otherwise acted in quite a friendly manner towards Harry Potter.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Hogwarts_years_(1991-1996)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years_.281991-1996.29">Hogwarts years <span class="template-c">(1991-1996)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1991-1996)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1991-1996)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="First_year">First year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: First year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>You know how I think they choose people for the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor team</a>. It's people they feel sorry for. See, there's Potter, who's got no parents, then there's the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasleys</a>, who've got no money — you should be on the team, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Longbottom</a>, you've got no brains.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco mocking Gryffindor students<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/95/SortingHat_WB_F1_DracoMalfoyInTheSortingHat_Still_100615_Land.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160718204423" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="SortingHat WB F1 DracoMalfoyInTheSortingHat Still 100615 Land.jpg" data-image-key="SortingHat_WB_F1_DracoMalfoyInTheSortingHat_Still_100615_Land.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/95/SortingHat_WB_F1_DracoMalfoyInTheSortingHat_Still_100615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160718204423" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/95/SortingHat_WB_F1_DracoMalfoyInTheSortingHat_Still_100615_Land.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160718204423" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/95/SortingHat_WB_F1_DracoMalfoyInTheSortingHat_Still_100615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160718204423" decoding="async" width="250" height="114" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="SortingHat WB F1 DracoMalfoyInTheSortingHat Still 100615 Land.jpg" data-image-key="SortingHat_WB_F1_DracoMalfoyInTheSortingHat_Still_100615_Land.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/95/SortingHat_WB_F1_DracoMalfoyInTheSortingHat_Still_100615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160718204423" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:SortingHat_WB_F1_DracoMalfoyInTheSortingHat_Still_100615_Land.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco being sorted into Slytherin House</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> for the very first time, Draco Malfoy offered his friendship to Harry Potter as his <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">father</a> believed that Harry was a Dark wizard, and Draco wished to impress him and relay some interesting news home. However, Harry didn't like the attitude Draco expressed towards <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, with whom Harry had already made friends, and also found that Draco reminded him of his cousin <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley</a>, with his disdainful attitude. Thus, he turned him down, creating animosity that lasted through the rest of their schooling.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Once at Hogwarts, Draco was Sorted into the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a>, like many other members of his family. He rapidly formed friendships with fellow Slytherins, while remaining hostile toward Harry to the point of challenging him to a <a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">duel</a>, after Harry beat him to Neville Longbottom's <a href="/wiki/Remembrall" title="Remembrall">Remembrall</a> during their first <a href="/wiki/Flying_(class)" title="Flying (class)">Flying lesson</a>. This was, in fact, an attempt to get Harry into trouble for being out after curfew. He resented the attention Harry received because of his fame and his prodigious flying ability, which led to Harry being permitted to join his house's <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_team" title="Quidditch team">team</a> at a younger age than most.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/WB_F1_Fang_HarryMalfoyFangInForest_11428.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170924160828" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="WB F1 Fang HarryMalfoyFangInForest 11428.jpg" data-image-key="WB_F1_Fang_HarryMalfoyFangInForest_11428.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/WB_F1_Fang_HarryMalfoyFangInForest_11428.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170924160828" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/WB_F1_Fang_HarryMalfoyFangInForest_11428.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170924160828" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/WB_F1_Fang_HarryMalfoyFangInForest_11428.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170924160828" decoding="async" width="245" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="WB F1 Fang HarryMalfoyFangInForest 11428.jpg" data-image-key="WB_F1_Fang_HarryMalfoyFangInForest_11428.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/WB_F1_Fang_HarryMalfoyFangInForest_11428.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170924160828" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:WB_F1_Fang_HarryMalfoyFangInForest_11428.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> with Harry Potter during their detention</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later in the year, Draco discovered Harry's plan to smuggle Hagrid's pet dragon <a href="/wiki/Norberta" title="Norberta">Norbert</a> out of the castle and informed <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a> of it, but was put in detention as well for being out past curfew. For his detention, Draco had to assist <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>, who had been caught shortly after smuggling Norbert out, as well as <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, who had tried to warn them about Draco, in finding a wounded <a href="/wiki/Unicorn" title="Unicorn">unicorn</a>. This was a task he greatly resented because he found it to be "servants' work". He and Harry witnessed <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>, inhabiting the body of <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>, drinking the <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_blood" title="Unicorn blood">blood</a> of a unicorn and ran away in fear leaving Harry behind.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_15-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the end of the school year, Draco was initially overjoyed that Slytherin was on course to win the <a href="/wiki/House_Cup" title="House Cup">House Cup</a> again, but was very dejected to see <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> win the cup once <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> awarded Harry, Ron, Hermione and Neville additional house points for their brave actions.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_15-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_year">Second year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Second year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Saint Potter, the Mudbloods' friend... He's another one with no proper wizard feeling, or he wouldn't go around with that jumped-up Granger Mudblood. And people think he's Slytherin's heir!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco on speculation that Harry is the Heir of Slytherin<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/Dracohp2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120623161509" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dracohp2.png" data-image-key="Dracohp2.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/Dracohp2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120623161509" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/Dracohp2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120623161509" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/Dracohp2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120623161509" decoding="async" width="180" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dracohp2.png" data-image-key="Dracohp2.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/65/Dracohp2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120623161509" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dracohp2.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco mocking Harry Potter in Flourish and Blotts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/66/Draco2hp2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120623161619" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco2hp2.png" data-image-key="Draco2hp2.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/66/Draco2hp2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120623161619" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/66/Draco2hp2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120623161619" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/66/Draco2hp2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120623161619" decoding="async" width="180" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco2hp2.png" data-image-key="Draco2hp2.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/66/Draco2hp2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120623161619" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco2hp2.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco as the new Slytherin Seeker</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before the start of his second year, Draco Malfoy was present at <a href="/wiki/Flourish_and_Blotts" title="Flourish and Blotts">Flourish and Blotts</a> the day Harry, the <a href="/wiki/Granger_family" title="Granger family">Grangers</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasleys</a> were shopping for <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>'s new Hogwarts textbooks. After Harry was given a free copy of books by Lockhart personally, Draco afterwards approached him to insult him, and after <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginevra Weasley</a> defended him, he mocked her as his girlfriend (unintentionally predicting the future). Draco's father <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> was also present, who met Harry for the first time, and also encountered Arthur Weasley, who he insulted for associating with Muggles, such as the Grangers. Arthur then attacked Lucius in an angry rage, prompting them all to leave the shop.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In his second year at Hogwarts, Draco attained the position of <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> <a href="/wiki/Slytherin_Quidditch_team" title="Slytherin Quidditch team">team</a>. His <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">father</a> bought the entire team new <a href="/wiki/Nimbus_2001" title="Nimbus 2001">Nimbus 2001s</a> because of this, though <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> openly speculated that this was in fact what got Draco on the team at all. Draco responded angrily to this accusation, and called Hermione a "<i>filthy little <a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a></i>," causing the Gryffindor Quidditch team to lash out at him; <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> tried to <a href="/wiki/Slug-Vomiting_Charm" class="mw-redirect" title="Slug-Vomiting Charm">curse him to vomit slugs</a>, but the spell backfired due to his broken wand, which Draco and his team found very amusing.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ironically, Draco was the reason why Slytherin lost to Gryffindor that year in Quidditch, because he was unaware that the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Snitch" title="Golden Snitch">Golden Snitch</a> was hovering inches above his own left ear--too busy insulting Harry Potter to notice. Harry took advantage of the lapse in concentration, allowing Gryffindor to win the match and Draco to be reprimanded by the team captain <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Flint" title="Marcus Flint">Marcus Flint</a> for his stupidity, which was witnessed by <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Draco4hp2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120623161921" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco4hp2.png" data-image-key="Draco4hp2.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Draco4hp2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120623161921" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Draco4hp2.png/revision/latest?cb=20120623161921" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Draco4hp2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120623161921" decoding="async" width="180" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco4hp2.png" data-image-key="Draco4hp2.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Draco4hp2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120623161921" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco4hp2.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco preparing to duel Harry Potter</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During a meeting of the short-lived <a href="/wiki/Duelling_Club" title="Duelling Club">Duelling Club</a> that year, Draco duelled Harry Potter. He <a href="/wiki/Snake_Summons_Spell" title="Snake Summons Spell">conjured a snake</a> after being encouraged by Professor Snape and was disappointed when Harry thwarted the attack by speaking to the serpent in <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parseltongue</a>. This led many students to suspect that Harry was the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Heir of Slytherin</a>, who had opened the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> and released a "<a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">monster</a>." This caused Draco to be upset that any one would actually think that "<i>saint Potter, the Mudbloods' friend</i>" could be the heir of Slytherin, which was something that he thought was completely ridiculous.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Harry_Ron_polyjuice2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160513040256" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Ron polyjuice2.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Ron_polyjuice2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Harry_Ron_polyjuice2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160513040256" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Harry_Ron_polyjuice2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160513040256" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Harry_Ron_polyjuice2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160513040256" decoding="async" width="245" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Ron polyjuice2.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Ron_polyjuice2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Harry_Ron_polyjuice2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160513040256" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Ron_polyjuice2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco unknowingly being interrogated by Harry Potter  and Ron Weasley</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry, Ron, and Hermione suspected that Draco might be the Heir, given his bigoted views on <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a> and his family's tradition of being Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a>. Hermione brewed <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> in the girls' third floor bathroom so that Harry and Ron were able to disguise themselves as <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a> respectively and enter the Slytherin common room. There, Draco unwittingly revealed through conversation that he was not the heir, nor did he know who it was. He did tell them that the Chamber had been opened fifty years ago and that he wished he could help the true heir.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>It was, in fact, Draco's own father who had schemed to get the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> opened by planting <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary">an old diary</a> of Tom Riddle's on first-year student <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, though his true target in this plot was her father <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur</a>. It does not appear that Draco was aware of this, as Lucius's instructions to his son that year were to "<i>keep his head down</i>." The diary was a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>, containing a piece of Voldemort's soul, and it was destroyed when Harry stabbed it with a Basilisk fang while in the chamber itself.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>  When <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Professor Sprout</a> and <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Madame Pomfrey</a> were applauded for bringing everyone who was petrified back to their normal ways, Draco did not clap for them, but instead gave them an evil snobbish look.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Third_year">Third year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Third year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Third year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Draco</b>: "<i>I'm afraid he won't be a teacher much longer. Father's not very happy about my injury...he's complained to the school governors. And to the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>. Father's got a lot of influence, you know. And a lasting injury like this...who knows if my arm'll ever be the same again?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>So that's why you're putting it on. To try and get Hagrid sacked.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Draco</b>: "<i>Well, </i>partly<i>, Potter. But there are other benefits too.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Discussion of Draco's injury in a <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> class<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Draco_Malfoyyy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090608163311" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="308" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco Malfoyyy.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoyyy.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Draco_Malfoyyy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090608163311" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Draco_Malfoyyy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090608163311" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Draco_Malfoyyy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090608163311" decoding="async" width="180" height="308" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco Malfoyyy.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoyyy.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Draco_Malfoyyy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090608163311" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_Malfoyyy.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco attending his first Care of Magical Creatures class in 1993</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Draco started off his <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">third year</a> by mocking <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>'s reaction to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> that were near Hogwarts that year searching for escaped <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> prisoner <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, despite being terrified of them himself. He also hinted at Black's crimes regarding Harry and his <a href="/wiki/James_and_Lily_Potter" title="James and Lily Potter">late parents</a>, which Harry was unaware of for some time, and told him that if someone had betrayed and gotten his parents killed  — as it was believed Black had done to the <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potters</a> — he would seek revenge.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a>, Draco, <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Flint" title="Marcus Flint">Marcus Flint</a> attempted to undermine Harry's performance by posing as <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> — Draco standing on Goyle's shoulders — but they were all knocked over by Harry's first successful automatic <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a>, clearly unaware that it was the effect the dementors had on Harry that he had a problem with rather than the dementors themselves. Their attempt to sabotage Harry's performance ended up costing the Slytherin House 50 points.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170808144851" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione punching Draco GIF.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20170808144851" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170808144851" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20170808144851" decoding="async" width="240" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione punching Draco GIF.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20170808144851" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> <a href="/wiki/Muggle_duelling" title="Muggle duelling">punches</a> Draco</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In a <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> lesson, Draco unintentionally provoked the <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">Hippogriff</a> <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>, and was injured, though he exaggerated how badly he was hurt for attention, and in an attempt to use the incident against <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> to get him fired. When Draco mocked him for how upset he became over the case, Hermione slapped Draco in anger. Lucius tried to get the creature executed, and although he was successful in obtaining this sentence, <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a> was saved through the efforts of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> with the help of a <a href="/wiki/Time-turner" class="mw-redirect" title="Time-turner">time-turner</a>, and given to <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Black</a> when his innocence was proven  to Harry, Ron and Hermione .<sup id="cite_ref-POA_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> This outcome angered both Draco and his father.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_year">Fourth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fourth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Fourth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Granger, they’re after Muggles, D’you want to be showing off your knickers in midair? Because if you do, hang around . . . they’re moving this way, and it would give us all a laugh.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco intimidating the <a href="/wiki/Trio" title="Trio">trio</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Reappearance_of_the_Dark_Mark" title="Reappearance of the Dark Mark">riot</a> at the Quidditch world cup<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Malfoys_in_Top_Box.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817203847" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Malfoys in Top Box.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoys_in_Top_Box.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Malfoys_in_Top_Box.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20190817203847" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Malfoys_in_Top_Box.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190817203847" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Malfoys_in_Top_Box.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20190817203847" decoding="async" width="245" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Malfoys in Top Box.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoys_in_Top_Box.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7c/Malfoys_in_Top_Box.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20190817203847" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Malfoys_in_Top_Box.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco with his father at the 1994 Quidditch World Cup</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, Draco attended the <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_World_Cup" title="Quidditch World Cup">Quidditch World Cup</a> with his parents. They sat in the <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>'s luxury box as guests of the Minister, due to <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius</a>'s large donation. He was seated directly behind trio and the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasleys</a>. He taunted <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> when a group of <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> began terrorising the campers after the game, mocking the <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a> they were tormenting and implying that they would do the same to Hermione because of her <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> status. Harry asked if his father (<a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>) was participating in the riot and he responded with a "wouldn't you like to know," as the answer was yes. Once on the train to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> Draco proceeded to mock the trio about their lack of knowledge regarding the upcoming school event.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/B4C18M1_Densaugeo_and_Furnunculus.png/revision/latest?cb=20161211010749" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="108" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C18M1 Densaugeo and Furnunculus.png" data-image-key="B4C18M1_Densaugeo_and_Furnunculus.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/B4C18M1_Densaugeo_and_Furnunculus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161211010749" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/B4C18M1_Densaugeo_and_Furnunculus.png/revision/latest?cb=20161211010749" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/B4C18M1_Densaugeo_and_Furnunculus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161211010749" decoding="async" width="250" height="108" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C18M1 Densaugeo and Furnunculus.png" data-image-key="B4C18M1_Densaugeo_and_Furnunculus.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/B4C18M1_Densaugeo_and_Furnunculus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161211010749" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C18M1_Densaugeo_and_Furnunculus.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco after unintentionally hitting Hermione with the <i>Densaugeo</i> hex during a short duel with Harry</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During his fourth year Hogwarts hosted the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, and, much to Draco's dismay and jealousy, Harry was chosen as a champion despite being too young. Draco supported <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a>, passing out badges that could be made to read <i>Potter Stinks</i> and taunting Harry regularly, such as commenting that he was betting Harry wouldn't last more than a few minutes with the <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">dragons</a>. He was proven wrong when Harry tied with Cedric for first place and succeeded in capturing his <a href="/wiki/Golden_egg" title="Golden egg">golden egg</a> the fastest.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was also the informer and impetus behind <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> writing slanderous, sensationalist articles about <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> for the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i>, due to him knowing that she was an <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">animagus</a>; this assault on Harry's credibility would set the stage for widespread disbelief of Harry's announcement that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> had returned at the end of the school year. Some of the articles that he was partly for was one about Harry and Hermione titled <i>Harry Potter's Secret Heartache</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/36/Malfoy_Ferret.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160315083146" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Malfoy Ferret.gif" data-image-key="Malfoy_Ferret.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/36/Malfoy_Ferret.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160315083146" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/36/Malfoy_Ferret.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160315083146" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/36/Malfoy_Ferret.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160315083146" decoding="async" width="250" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Malfoy Ferret.gif" data-image-key="Malfoy_Ferret.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/36/Malfoy_Ferret.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160315083146" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Malfoy_Ferret.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> (disguised as Professor <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Moody</a>) scaring Draco Malfoy by transfiguring him into a ferret</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Draco tried to cast a <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy%27s_unspecified_spell" title="Draco Malfoy&#39;s unspecified spell">spell</a> at Harry early in the year behind his back, the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch Junior</a> (disguised as <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> using <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>) <a href="/wiki/Ferret_to_human_spell" title="Ferret to human spell">transformed</a> Draco into a <a href="/wiki/Ferret" title="Ferret">ferret</a> and bounced him around the room as punishment. Although <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a> stopped it, Draco was very embarrassed and other students were highly amused; Ron dubbed him "<i>the Amazing Bouncing Ferret</i>". Throughout the year, students would tease Draco by telling him that <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Professor Moody</a> was behind him, causing him to flinch or shudder. Even Hagrid noted that he had heard that Draco had made a good ferret, making Draco not know what to say. At <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas</a> time, Draco attended the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> with <a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the end of the year, Draco mocked Harry about his choice to side against Voldemort and also ridiculed <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a>'s death. Before he could finish, however, he was hit by several <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curses</a> from Harry, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fred_and_George_Weasley" title="Fred and George Weasley">Fred and George Weasley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_3-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fifth_year">Fifth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fifth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Fifth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>The <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a>... A select group of students who are supportive of the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, hand-picked by <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Professor Umbridge</a>. Members of the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a> do have the power to dock points... So, Granger, I’ll have five from you for being rude about our new headmistress... <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Macmillan" title="Ernest Macmillan">Macmillan</a>, five for contradicting me... Five because I don’t like you, Potter... Weasley, your shirt's untucked, so I’ll have another five for that... Oh yeah, I forgot, you’re a Mudblood, Granger, so ten for that...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco as a member of the Inquisitorial Squad<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>In 1995, Draco became a <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> along with <a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a>. He was sure to mock <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> for not receiving the same honour, as <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a>'s prefects were <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>. He also wrote the lyrics to the demeaning song <i><a href="/wiki/Weasley_is_Our_King" title="Weasley is Our King">Weasley is Our King</a></i>, which mocked Ron's Quidditch abilities as Gryffindor <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a>. It was the invention of this song, as well as insulting <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly</a> and <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> and the late <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a> to Harry, Fred, and George's faces that prompted Harry and George to get into a fight with Draco. They violently assaulted him, which resulted in the pair (as well as George's twin brother Fred) being banned from all further <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> matches, although their bans were later lifted after <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>'s sacking from <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> and her being put on suspension for her actions.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/42/Draco2hp5.png/revision/latest?cb=20170721023740" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco2hp5.png" data-image-key="Draco2hp5.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/42/Draco2hp5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170721023740" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/42/Draco2hp5.png/revision/latest?cb=20170721023740" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/42/Draco2hp5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170721023740" decoding="async" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco2hp5.png" data-image-key="Draco2hp5.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/42/Draco2hp5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170721023740" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco2hp5.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Malfoy joins Dolores Umbridge's Inquisitorial Squad</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later that year, he joined Umbridge's <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a>, and clearly enjoyed the power this gave him over other students. He held this power over Harry and his friends especially. All of the Squad members were Slytherins, as Umbridge was bias and favoured students of her former house. Draco caught Harry running out of the last meeting of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, receiving fifty house points, for Slytherin, from Umbridge.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, he was among the Inquisitorial Squad members who caught Harry and his friends in their attempt to discover the whereabouts of <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, whom Harry had seen being tortured in a vision, planted by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>. Harry, Ron, Hermione, <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> were all brought to Umbridge's office, guarded by the Inquisitorial Squad. Before Umbridge could carry through on her threat to use the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> to make Harry talk, Hermione told Umbridge that they were trying to contact <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> about a "weapon" that he planned to use against the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>. Draco had an expression of "eagerness and greed" at this news that convinced Umbridge not to allow him or any other Squad member to accompany her as she took Harry and Hermione into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> in search of the alleged weapon.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161216060209" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg" data-image-key="InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161216060209" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161216060209" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161216060209" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg" data-image-key="InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161216060209" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Inquisitorial Squad holds several D.A. members hostage for Umbridge</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Umbridge left, the remaining D.A. (Dumbledore's Army) members used a litany of <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spells</a> and <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charms</a> to escape the office; Draco was hit by Ginny's <a href="/wiki/Bat-Bogey_Hex" title="Bat-Bogey Hex">Bat-Bogey Hex</a>. It was soon revealed that Hermione had been lying about a weapon; Umbridge was carried off by <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaurs</a> and the six D.A. members flew to the Ministry, where the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> ensued.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_17-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Draco's father was seen participating in the battle as a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> and was imprisoned in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for his crimes. Draco was very upset by this, and mainly blamed Harry, swearing vengeance and attempting to attack him at the end of the school year with the help of <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>. However, other <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">D.A.</a> members came to Harry's defence, resulting in Draco, Crabbe, and Goyle ending up looking like ugly slug-like things after being hit by a number of hexes by all D.A. Members at the same time.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_17-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sixth_year">Sixth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sixth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Sixth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Wow... look at that... he’s not here now! So why not have a go? They might be able to find you a double cell in Azkaban with your loser of a husband!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Draco</b>: "<i>Don’t you dare talk to my mother like that, Potter!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Narcissa Malfoy</b>: "<i>It’s all right, Draco. I expect Potter will be reunited with dear <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a> before I am reunited with Lucius.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Draco and his mother argue against Harry in <a href="/wiki/Madam_Malkin%27s_Robes_for_All_Occasions" title="Madam Malkin&#39;s Robes for All Occasions">Madam Malkin's</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2897.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150805161658" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2897.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2897.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2897.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805161658" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2897.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150805161658" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2897.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805161658" decoding="async" width="250" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2897.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2897.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2897.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805161658" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2897.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco talking to <a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a> and <a href="/wiki/Blaise_Zabini" title="Blaise Zabini">Blaise Zabini</a> on the Hogwarts express about his mission from Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>By late <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Draco joined the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, having replaced his incarcerated <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">father</a>. He bragged about having been given a mission to his fellow <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> students on his way to school on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>. However, as the year dragged on, Draco became increasingly afraid that he would fail in his seemingly impossible task — to kill <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. It is implied that Draco was expected to fail and that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> assigned him the task with the intention of punishing <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> for his failure at the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a>. The safety of his family rested on Draco's success with his mission. When Harry overhead some parts of Draco's conversation with his fellow Slytherins about the mission, Draco used a <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a> to paralyse Harry and stomped hard on his face, crushing his nose, in revenge for imprisoning his father, Lucius, causing Harry to hate Draco more than ever, while disregarding what Harry heard as not important enough to condemn him.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Draco planned to repair a <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts-Borgin_and_Burkes_Vanishing_Cabinet_pair" title="Hogwarts-Borgin and Burkes Vanishing Cabinet pair">Vanishing Cabinet</a> that <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> had destroyed four years previously, in order to smuggle <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> into <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> to assist him in killing Dumbledore. In his previous year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> a fellow <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Graham_Montague" title="Graham Montague">Graham Montague</a>, had been forced into it by the <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Weasley</a> <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">twins</a> and later managed to <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">apparate</a> out as a last resort to free himself from the limbo-like space into which he had vanished. Montague told Draco that during his time trapped in limbo, he could hear the sounds entering the cabinet from the school, as well as the sounds entering the cabinet's twin in <a href="/wiki/Borgin_and_Burkes" title="Borgin and Burkes">Borgin and Burkes</a>. Draco realised from this that if the broken one was repaired, the cabinets could act as a passageway into the school.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/12/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2485.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150805163109" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2485.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2485.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/12/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2485.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805163109" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/12/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2485.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150805163109" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/12/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2485.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805163109" decoding="async" width="250" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2485.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2485.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/12/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2485.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805163109" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-2485.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco preparing to enter <a href="/wiki/Borgin_and_Burkes" title="Borgin and Burkes">Borgin and Burkes</a>, wanting to question Borgin</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the summer break between his fifth and sixth year, Draco questioned Borgin, the owner of Borgin and Burkes, on repairing the cabinet and ordered him to keep the other one safe. As a proof of his allegiance to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, Draco showed Borgin the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a> now branded on his arm whilst threatening to set <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> to attack the shop-owner, should he disobey his commands.
