This meeting was also overheard by Harry, Hermione, and Ron, but while Harry started to suspect Draco of <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> activities, Ron and Hermione dismissed such possibilities, and believed Draco was merely bluffing, a choice that they would much later regret.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In preparation for such a dangerous mission, Draco trained and improved his own skills, and became capable of blocking jinxes <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">nonverbally</a>. He also became accomplished at <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> through the training of his maternal aunt <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, and was able to perform the very difficult <a href="/wiki/Protean_Charm" title="Protean Charm">Protean Charm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> though he could not yet produce a corporeal <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a5/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-5267.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150805162606" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="116" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-5267.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-5267.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a5/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-5267.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805162606" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a5/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-5267.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150805162606" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a5/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-5267.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805162606" decoding="async" width="250" height="116" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-5267.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-5267.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a5/Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-5267.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150805162606" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-half-blood-movie-screencaps.com-5267.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco standing in front of the broken Vanishing Cabinet</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In focus for his mission of fixing the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts-Borgin_and_Burkes_Vanishing_Cabinet_pair" title="Hogwarts-Borgin and Burkes Vanishing Cabinet pair">Vanishing Cabinet</a>, Draco experienced many visible changes in his life. He seemed to have lost interest in <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a>, and allowed (and possibly paid) <a href="/wiki/Harper" title="Harper">Harper</a> to take over instead. He was also becoming more neglectful in his school-work, as he missed two <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> homework assignments and received detention, as well as not attending to his <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> duties, which he would usually happily abuse as he did in the previous year. Another change was that he no longer trusted <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Snape</a> and was willing to speak ill towards him point-blank, no respect. Socially, Draco forced <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Crabbe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Goyle</a> to assume the forms of other people with <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>, to help him keep watch outside the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>, while refusing to tell them anything, and seemingly to distance himself from them. Draco also spent less time mocking Harry and his friends, despite the many opportunities. Even his physical appearance showed the stress, with greying skin, weight loss and bags under his eyes. Most of this frustrated Harry, who was unable to discover exactly what Draco was up to despite his persistence and effort.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 241px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Draco_Malfoy_mirror.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081115203903" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="239" height="116" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy mirror.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_mirror.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Draco_Malfoy_mirror.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/239?cb=20081115203903" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Draco_Malfoy_mirror.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081115203903" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Draco_Malfoy_mirror.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/239?cb=20081115203903" decoding="async" width="239" height="116" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy mirror.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_mirror.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Draco_Malfoy_mirror.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/239?cb=20081115203903" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_Malfoy_mirror.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco begins to feel the strain of life as a Death Eater</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Twice during the school year he feared he would be unable to repair the cabinet, and resorted to desperate assassination attempts, such as trying to smuggle in a cursed necklace and trying to send Dumbledore poisoned mead. Both these attempts failed and resulted in innocent people getting injured, though since they both survived Dumbledore was not forced to apprehend Draco. The stress began to affect Draco adversely, and he confessed his fears to <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Myrtle Warren</a>, one of the school's <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">ghosts</a>. On one such occasion, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> stumbled on him. Draco reacted by starting to cast the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>, but Harry <a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">sliced his skin open with his wand</a> right before he could complete the incantation. Draco was hospitalised and Harry was given detention by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Snape</a> for every Saturday until the end of term.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/29/Sectumsempra_Draco_2.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20180720154620" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sectumsempra Draco 2.JPG" data-image-key="Sectumsempra_Draco_2.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/29/Sectumsempra_Draco_2.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720154620" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/29/Sectumsempra_Draco_2.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20180720154620" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/29/Sectumsempra_Draco_2.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720154620" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sectumsempra Draco 2.JPG" data-image-key="Sectumsempra_Draco_2.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/29/Sectumsempra_Draco_2.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720154620" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sectumsempra_Draco_2.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry nearly kills Draco with one of Snape's spells</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Eventually, through copious amounts of work Draco managed to repair <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts-Borgin_and_Burkes_Vanishing_Cabinet_pair" title="Hogwarts-Borgin and Burkes Vanishing Cabinet pair">the Vanishing Cabinet</a> and used it to let at least six Death Eaters into the castle: Corban Yaxley, Alecto Carrow, Amycus Carrow, Gibbon, Thorfin Rowle, and the vicious werewolf <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>. Proceeding to the top of the <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_Tower" title="Astronomy Tower">Astronomy Tower</a>, Draco was able to corner a significantly weaker <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, disarming the latter the same instant he had, unknown to Draco, bound Harry Potter with a <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>However, when Draco was finally given the opportunity to kill Dumbledore, who had just expressed his willingness to protect Draco and his family were they to "come over to the right side," he could not bring himself to commit murder; considering that they spent the few minutes of alone time to discuss how Draco smuggled his accomplices into the castle, Dumbledore concluded that Draco would find committing murder impossible. As predicted, Draco ultimately was unable to do it, instead lowering his wand. Snape, who had made an <a href="/wiki/Unbreakable_Vow" title="Unbreakable Vow">Unbreakable Vow</a> with Narcissa to step in if Draco failed in his task, used the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. Snape then promptly led Draco out of the school grounds, presumably to safety, but really to get to a safe distance to disapparate to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Draco disarmed Dumbledore, he unknowingly gained the allegiance of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>, one of the three <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/20/Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007223528" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="109" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco disarms dumbledore.gif" data-image-key="Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/20/Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20161007223528" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/20/Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007223528" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/20/Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20161007223528" decoding="async" width="245" height="109" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco disarms dumbledore.gif" data-image-key="Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/20/Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20161007223528" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_disarms_dumbledore.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco disarms Albus Dumbledore on top of the Astronomy Tower</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, Draco could no longer return to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, as he was an accomplice, however reluctantly, in the revered <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>'s murder, mainly by being the one who let Death Eaters penetrate the castle's walls. The official criminal status placed on him, alongside his fear of the Dark Lord's wrath, led him to seek refuge, along with his family, with Voldemort, in the hopes of satisfying his orders to prevent any more negative highlights.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His abrupt departure from the school left <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a> surprisingly lonely, despite the two being hulking boys, as Harry described during Dumbledore's funeral.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Seventh_year">Seventh year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Seventh year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Seventh year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor"><a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Skirmish at Malfoy Manor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>I can’t — I can’t be sure.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco's refusal to identify Harry Potter in Malfoy Manor<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 248px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Malfoy_Manor_interrogation.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141222191729" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="246" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Malfoy Manor interrogation.gif" data-image-key="Malfoy_Manor_interrogation.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Malfoy_Manor_interrogation.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20141222191729" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Malfoy_Manor_interrogation.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141222191729" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Malfoy_Manor_interrogation.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20141222191729" decoding="async" width="246" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Malfoy Manor interrogation.gif" data-image-key="Malfoy_Manor_interrogation.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/Malfoy_Manor_interrogation.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20141222191729" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Malfoy_Manor_interrogation.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco ambiguously recognises Harry when he is brought to Lord Voldemort's headquarters by Snatchers</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Draco reluctantly participated in Death Eater activities before the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/1997%E2%80%931998_school_year" title="1997–1998 school year">1997–1998 school year</a>. Due to Draco's helpful role in Dumbledore's death, Voldemort liberated Lucius from Azkaban. He witnessed the murder of <a href="/wiki/Charity_Burbage" title="Charity Burbage">Charity Burbage</a> and tortured <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a> on Lord Voldemort's orders. Judging by later remarks made by Vincent Crabbe, it seems that the Malfoys had lost much of their influence in the Death Eater circles. This is due to Voldemort no longer holding Lucius in high esteem and shifting his favour to Draco's maternal aunt Bellatrix Lestrange and Hogwarts teacher Severus Snape.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Draco attended his seventh year of Hogwarts that year. During the <a href="/wiki/Easter" title="Easter">Easter holidays</a>, Draco was seen at home in <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>. He was called upon by his parents and aunt <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> to confirm the identities of Harry, Ron and Hermione, who were caught by a group of <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a> led by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>, but Draco showed great hesitation in doing so. When Hermione lied to Bellatrix under <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">torture</a> about <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's Sword</a>, Draco was sent to fetch the <a href="/wiki/Goblin" title="Goblin">goblin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Griphook" title="Griphook">Griphook</a>, from the dungeons to get confirmation of the story, which he did by lying saying it was a fake, but the truth was it was the true sword. Later in the evening, the prisoners managed to escape, and <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy%27s_wand" title="Draco Malfoy&#39;s wand">Draco's wand</a> was taken by Harry. Afterwards, Draco and his family were detained to the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Manor</a> by Lord Voldemort. Narcissa would lend Draco <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy%27s_wand" title="Narcissa Malfoy&#39;s wand">her wand</a>; it was powerful, yet it didn't "understand" him, as he had not won its loyalty.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Draco Malfoy</b>: "<i>STOP! The <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Dark Lord</a> wants <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">him</a> alive —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Vincent Crabbe</b>: "<i>So? I'm not killing him, am I? But if I can, I will, the Dark Lord wants him <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">dead</a> anyway, what's the diff —&#160;?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Draco Malfoy</b>: "<i>Don't kill him! DON'T KILL HIM!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Draco tries to control his cohorts in the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 236px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/HPDH2-04075r-900x600.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110707090451" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="234" height="156" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HPDH2-04075r-900x600.jpg" data-image-key="HPDH2-04075r-900x600.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/HPDH2-04075r-900x600.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/234?cb=20110707090451" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/HPDH2-04075r-900x600.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110707090451" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/HPDH2-04075r-900x600.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/234?cb=20110707090451" decoding="async" width="234" height="156" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HPDH2-04075r-900x600.jpg" data-image-key="HPDH2-04075r-900x600.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/HPDH2-04075r-900x600.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/234?cb=20110707090451" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HPDH2-04075r-900x600.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco with his parents during the second-half of the Battle of Hogwarts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later that same year, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Draco, along with Crabbe and Goyle, chose to remain in the school as their fellow Slytherins evacuated in order to bring Harry Potter to Lord Voldemort. Given Lucius' previous remarks alluding to "forgiveness", it is likely that Draco was doing this in an attempt to redeem his family in Voldemort's eyes. He along with Crabbe and Goyle followed the Trio into the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> where he would attempt to capture Harry and retrieve the item Harry was trying to locate. However, he no longer exercised the same degree of control over his friends, particularly Crabbe, that he once had.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Harry_and_Draco.png/revision/latest?cb=20170204081554" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry and Draco.png" data-image-key="Harry_and_Draco.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Harry_and_Draco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170204081554" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Harry_and_Draco.png/revision/latest?cb=20170204081554" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Harry_and_Draco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170204081554" decoding="async" width="250" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry and Draco.png" data-image-key="Harry_and_Draco.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Harry_and_Draco.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170204081554" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_and_Draco.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry saves Draco from Fiendfye in the Room of Requirement</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite Draco telling his friends that Harry was to be brought back alive, Crabbe attempted to kill him by conjuring <a href="/wiki/Fiendfyre" title="Fiendfyre">Fiendfyre</a>. Since Crabbe was unable to control the curse, the Room of Requirement quickly filled with fire. Draco went out of his way to try to save both of his friends, but he only managed to get Goyle, who had been <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stunned</a> by Hermione during the fight, onto Ron and Hermione's broom before he let Harry fly them out. Crabbe was killed in the fire, leaving Draco very upset.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Harry, Hermione, and Ron later spotted Draco pleading with a Death Eater that he was on his side. Harry <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stunned</a> the Death Eater and Ron <a href="/wiki/Muggle_duelling" title="Muggle duelling">punched</a> Draco and called him a "<i>two-faced bastard</i>", as this was the second time they saved his life that night.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Although Draco was unaware of this, his act in disarming Dumbledore before his death and mastering the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> ultimately resulted in the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Lord</a>'s final defeat at the hands of Harry. This is due to the fact that Voldemort was unable to fully understand the Elder Wand's power and Harry disarming Draco of his wand resulted in him mastering the Elder Wand himself.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Voldemort's defeat, Draco and his parents sat in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>, looking uncertain of their place during the victory celebrations.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="After_Hogwarts_(1998-2006)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="After_Hogwarts_.281998-2006.29">After Hogwarts <span class="template-c">(1998-2006)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: After Hogwarts (1998-2006)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: After Hogwarts (1998-2006)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Draco_Malfoy_Older_Cursed_Child.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20160924184520" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="187" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy Older Cursed Child.jpeg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_Older_Cursed_Child.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Draco_Malfoy_Older_Cursed_Child.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160924184520" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Draco_Malfoy_Older_Cursed_Child.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20160924184520" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Draco_Malfoy_Older_Cursed_Child.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160924184520" decoding="async" width="180" height="187" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy Older Cursed Child.jpeg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_Older_Cursed_Child.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Draco_Malfoy_Older_Cursed_Child.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160924184520" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_Malfoy_Older_Cursed_Child.jpeg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">An adult Draco</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The events of Draco's teenage years forever changed his life.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> He had the beliefs in which he had grown up challenged in the most frightening way, had experienced terror and despair, witnessed his parents suffering for their allegiance, and had witnessed the crumbling of all that his family had believed in.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Draco and his family avoided imprisonment in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> due to their last-minute switch in allegiance. <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius</a> found his son as affectionate as ever, but refusing to follow the old pure-blood line.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Draco eventually married <a href="/wiki/Astoria_Malfoy" title="Astoria Malfoy">Astoria Greengrass</a>, the younger sister of fellow <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> classmate <a href="/wiki/Daphne_Greengrass" title="Daphne Greengrass">Daphne Greengrass</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> who had gone through a similar (though less violent and frightening) conversion from pure-blood ideals to a more accepting and tolerant way of life. This was something of a disappointment for Lucius and Narcissa, who had higher hopes of someone whose family featured on the "<a href="/wiki/Sacred_Twenty-Eight" title="Sacred Twenty-Eight">Sacred Twenty-Eight</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Raising_Scorpius_Malfoy_(2006-)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Raising_Scorpius_Malfoy_.282006-.29">Raising Scorpius Malfoy <span class="template-c">(2006-)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Raising Scorpius Malfoy (2006-)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Raising Scorpius Malfoy (2006-)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/dc/Draco_Scorpius.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160802023014" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="116" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco Scorpius.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Scorpius.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/dc/Draco_Scorpius.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160802023014" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/dc/Draco_Scorpius.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160802023014" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/dc/Draco_Scorpius.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160802023014" decoding="async" width="180" height="116" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco Scorpius.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Scorpius.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/dc/Draco_Scorpius.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160802023014" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_Scorpius.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco with his son Scorpius</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The two had a son together, named <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a>, who was raised by his mother not to believe that <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a> and <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a> were scum; as such, family gatherings were fraught with tension.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Draco raised Scorpius to be a much kinder and more accepting Malfoy than he was in his youth.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200621194235" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Malfoys on Platform Nine and Three-Quarters.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20200621194235" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200621194235" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20200621194235" decoding="async" width="235" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Malfoys on Platform Nine and Three-Quarters.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20200621194235" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco with his wife and son in 2017</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/1_September" title="1 September">1 September</a>, <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a> while sending his son off for his first year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, Draco greeted <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> at <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Cross_Station" title="King&#39;s Cross Station">King's Cross Station</a> with a curt nod. The relationship between Harry and Draco was much better than it had been when they were students together, but they were still not considered to be anything at all near friends.
</p><p>Independently wealthy without any need to work, Draco inhabited <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a> with his wife and son. His hobbies — which included keeping the family's old collection of <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark</a> artefacts (which he did not use and kept in glass cases) and studying <a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">alchemical</a> manuscripts — were indications of his dual nature, and hint at a desire for something more than wealth.<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Draco also teamed up with his former enemies to <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_St_Jerome%27s_Church" title="Skirmish at St Jerome&#39;s Church">fight</a> <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a> at <a href="/wiki/St_Jerome%27s_Church" title="St Jerome&#39;s Church">St Jerome's Church</a> in order to stop her from preventing Lord Voldemort's death.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Physical appearance"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623200347" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="274" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy (HBP promo).jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_(HBP_promo).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623200347" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623200347" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623200347" decoding="async" width="180" height="274" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy (HBP promo).jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_(HBP_promo).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623200347" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_Malfoy_(HBP_promo).jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco Malfoy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Draco was a slender boy with sleek white-blond hair, cold grey eyes, a pale complexion and rather sharp, pointed features.<sup id="cite_ref-face_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-face-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-face2_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-face2-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He was described to have haughty good looks. As an older man, his hairline was receding, making his features look even more pointed.<sup id="cite_ref-DH-E_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-E-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> In his first and second years he had blonde hair slicked tightly back. Draco is noted to strongly resemble his <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">father</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> When Draco joined the Death Eaters, Lord Voldemort had the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a> burned into his left forearm, which has since faded to a mere scar upon Voldemort's death.
</p><p>During the first five years of school Draco maintained a relatively healthy look. However, in his sixth year onward, when the stress of his mission was getting more intense, Draco's smug countenance was lost, and he became quite thin, with dark shadows under his eyes and a greyish tinge to his skin.
</p><p>As an adult, Draco let his hair grow long and started wearing it in a precisely placed ponytail.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>You've picked the losing side, Potter! I warned you! I told you you ought to choose your company more carefully, remember? When we met on the train, first day at Hogwarts? I told you not to hang around with riff-raff like this! Too late now, Potter! They’ll be the first to go, now the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Dark Lord</a>'s back! <a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudbloods</a> and <a href="/wiki/Blood_traitor" title="Blood traitor">Muggle-lovers</a> first! Well — second — <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Diggory</a> was the first —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco taunting <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> after Voldemort's return and the murder of Cedric Diggory<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Chamber-of-secrets-draco.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180523035744" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="249" height="133" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Chamber-of-secrets-draco.jpg" data-image-key="Chamber-of-secrets-draco.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Chamber-of-secrets-draco.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20180523035744" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Chamber-of-secrets-draco.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180523035744" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Chamber-of-secrets-draco.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20180523035744" decoding="async" width="249" height="133" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Chamber-of-secrets-draco.jpg" data-image-key="Chamber-of-secrets-draco.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Chamber-of-secrets-draco.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20180523035744" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Chamber-of-secrets-draco.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco's arrogant demeanour</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>  
<p>Draco was, in general, an arrogant, spiteful bully for most of his early years. Like <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley Dursley</a>, his narcissistic nature most likely stemmed from his being spoiled by his parents throughout his childhood, though according to Harry himself, Draco was even less sympathetic than his cousin. He believed himself superior to most people because of his family's pure-blood lineage as well as great wealth and social standing. He frequently behaved cruelly to Muggle-borns, so-called blood traitors, <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> students, and anyone who was a supporter of Harry Potter or <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. For much of his youth, Draco took after his bigoted father, <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, as a role model, and frequently boasted about his family's influence and wealth.
</p><p>Draco was intelligent, cunning and quick-witted, capable of deducing things and coming up with clever plans based on a small amount of information; his father had expected him to obtain top marks in school after his first year, and showed disappointment that Hermione beat him. He figured out through Montague's experience that <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts-Borgin_and_Burkes_Vanishing_Cabinet_pair" title="Hogwarts-Borgin and Burkes Vanishing Cabinet pair">the Vanishing Cabinets</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> and <a href="/wiki/Borgin_and_Burkes" title="Borgin and Burkes">Borgin and Burkes</a> were linked and that he could use that passage to his advantage. However, his plans could have limitations based on his own arrogance when dealing with people. When he attempted to sabotage Harry during the Gryffindor-Ravenclaw Quidditch match in their third year, his whole plan was based solely around the idea that the Dementors' appearance scared Harry, ignorant of the fact that it was the effect the Dementors had on him that caused Harry problems. Draco was also adept at compartmentalising his emotions, as is evidenced in his success with <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/BroodingMalfoy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080706135744" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="BroodingMalfoy.jpg" data-image-key="BroodingMalfoy.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/BroodingMalfoy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080706135744" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/BroodingMalfoy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080706135744" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/BroodingMalfoy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080706135744" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="BroodingMalfoy.jpg" data-image-key="BroodingMalfoy.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/BroodingMalfoy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080706135744" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:BroodingMalfoy.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco in his sixth year</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, something began to change in Draco's psyche in his sixth year at Hogwarts. After <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> made him a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>, he gave Draco the task of assassinating <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> by the end of the year, something that Draco was very eager to do at first. After a number of feeble attempts, Draco began to crack under the enormous pressure that Voldemort was putting on him. He was uncertain of his ability to fulfil the mission and was terrified that he and his family would pay the price for his failure; the stress led him to be reckless as his two feeble attempts were noted to be foolish by Snape, and he attempted a <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on Harry, despite the consequences of a life sentence in Azkaban.
</p><p>Over the course of the year, the mission also led Draco to neglect other aspects of his school life that he would previously have abused or enjoyed: he rejected his Prefect duties that he once would happily abuse; he feigned illness and paid another student to take over his stead in order to avoid playing Quidditch himself, as opposed to three years earlier when he would ensure the entire match was postponed by exaggerating a minor injury in order to suit the team's interest; he missed two Transfiguration homework assignments; he would distance himself from his friends Crabbe and Goyle and order them to be on lookout without telling them anything; and he would also spend less time mocking Harry and his friends despite the many opportunities. Ultimately, Draco was unable to kill Dumbledore, lowering his wand and being tempted to take Dumbledore's offer of protection for his parents.
</p><p>For the rest of the Second Wizarding War, Draco became disillusioned by the Death Eater lifestyle. He reluctantly participated in Death Eater activities and by the end of the war, remained on the fence. When <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> were captured in his home, Draco showed great hesitation in identifying them before the Death Eaters. Also, during the Battle of Hogwarts, he showed genuine concern for Crabbe and Goyle, something he rarely did.
</p><p>By the time Draco become an adult, he had became a noticeably changed man, due to his regret over joining the Death Eaters and the vile deeds he had to perform, even if only limited compared to his parents, and any of his old bigotry was lost, refusing to follow in line with the old pure-blood beliefs after having seen first-hand what happened to him and his parents for that. Due to this, he fell deeply in love with <a href="/wiki/Astoria_Malfoy" title="Astoria Malfoy">Astoria Malfoy</a> despite the disappointments of his parents over her failing to meet their hopes of someone from one of the <a href="/wiki/Sacred_Twenty-Eight" title="Sacred Twenty-Eight">Sacred Twenty-Eight</a>. As a husband, Draco was very loving and devoted and was fully willing to even let the Malfoy bloodline end to protect her from her family's curse as it made childbirth dangerous and detrimental to her health, which he maintained even despite Lucius's dislike, only relenting after Astoria said she wanted to leave behind a child for him and not for family beliefs. His wisdom shone by the fact that even though the temptation of using his family's secret Time Turner to see his wife just for one more minute was admittedly great, his respect for her desires and memory were too great to risk jeopardising the timeline for his beloved, showing how deeply Draco had fallen in love with her, as even though he had the power to alter time to be with her, he was able to, even if barely, resist such overwhelming temptation, showing how much his character had changed by the age of forty.
</p><p>Although <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius</a>'s birth would cause Astoria's death, Draco's love for his son was clearly great, considering the day he was born the greatest day of his life. Having seen how his parents spoiled him had caused him to become such a horrible man in his younger days, Draco strove to do better and henceforth he raised his son to be a better person. He did not let his histories with Harry, Ron and Hermione hamper his judgement towards Scorpius's bond with <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a> and crush on <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose Granger-Weasley</a>, children of his former rivals, fully supporting his son instead. His love for Scorpius was shown by how he showed no hesitation to give any Malfoy Family objects to his rivals if it would help in his son being found. In fact, he actually trusted Albus greatly, as he allowed him to connect with Scorpius when he couldn't after Astoria died, and genuinely care for the boy for what he meant to his son. Draco even went as far as to protest to Harry for having made Albus distant from Scorpius, showing how much he valued the friendship between Albus and Scorpius. Draco was more strict with Scorpius than his parents were to him, accepting that his son must be punished for having brought the wizarding world back to the times where Voldemort was in power. 
</p><p>His personal relationships with his old school rivals has also changed from antagonistic to being civil and tolerating. While he continued to mock Harry's friends for them only being so popular because of Harry and didn't trust them fully with matters regarding his son, as he gave a cold reply letter to Ginny's offer to having Scorpius stay in the Potter House, particularly being enraged at them for the rumours that Scorpius was Voldemort's son, he was more than willing to team up with Harry, Ron and Hermione to save both Albus and Scorpius and worked with them effectively to dispatch <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a>, despite her being the daughter of Voldemort and his aunt Bellatrix. This defiance of Delphini showed that even having the Dark Lord's daughter being a blood relative was a repugnant notion to Draco, wanting little to do with his Death Eater past, further shown by how he would attend and help his rivals in defeating what remained of the forces of darkness. By this time, Draco also began referring to Voldemort by his name rather than the "Dark Lord" as he did in his youth due to his self-redemption. He had came to trust the luck and instincts of both Harry and Hermione, taking the orders of the Minister For Magic without hesitation, even expressing he was impressed with her battle commands, albeit in a mildly amused manner, acknowledging Harry was always ready to solve the thickest of situations, and he even went as far as to confess to Harry that he never truly craved power like his father and that his ambition was actually to become a star Quidditch player, but he wasn't good enough, and mainly he just wanted to be happy along with the truth of Astoria's death,<sup id="cite_ref-CC442_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC442-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> and his envy of Harry's friendships, as he only ever had Crabbe and Goyle, outright acknowledging Harry as a friend and showing respect for him, which was mutually returned by Harry.<sup id="cite_ref-CC215_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC215-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Draco was a talented <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> from a young age and possessed several impressive <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magical</a> abilities. His wand was made of <a href="/wiki/Hawthorn" title="Hawthorn">hawthorn</a>, which one should only ever consider placing in the hands of a witch or wizard of proven talent. Following his training from his aunt <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, Draco grew to be an accomplished wizard for his age.
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">Love</a></b>: Although not a prominent ability for Draco, it should be noted that he was one of the few <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> who was capable of genuine love. He deeply cared about both his parents to the point that he would protect and defend them when necessary. His ability to love was more prominent later on in life, giving him the strength to abandon his old prejudice against non-pure bloods after seeing how much damage and devastation it caused to his family. This was evident as he raised his <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">son</a> away from that prejudice to be a better person than him and maintained a more civil relationship with his old school rivals to the point that he trusted their instincts while they searched for <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus</a> and Scorpius. He even claimed that he would have willingly ended the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoy bloodline</a> with himself if it meant protecting his <a href="/wiki/Astoria_Malfoy" title="Astoria Malfoy">wife</a>. Even though Draco disliked <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Professor Dumbledore</a> at the time, he was also extremely reluctant to kill Dumbledore despite being ordered by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> to do so in order to keep his family safe.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a></b>: In his sixth year, his Aunt <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix</a> taught him Occlumency to prepare him for his mission. As Draco had already shut down his compassion to become the bully he was, it was much easier for him to close his mind and disassociate from his emotions. He had enough skill in Occlumency that he was able to block out Severus Snape's (a powerful Legilimens) attempts to read his mind.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2f/The_Trio_%28Crabbe%2C_Malfoy_and_Goyle%29_1991b.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20180607063603" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Trio (Crabbe, Malfoy and Goyle) 1991b.JPG" data-image-key="The_Trio_(Crabbe,_Malfoy_and_Goyle)_1991b.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2f/The_Trio_%28Crabbe%2C_Malfoy_and_Goyle%29_1991b.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180607063603" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2f/The_Trio_%28Crabbe%2C_Malfoy_and_Goyle%29_1991b.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20180607063603" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2f/The_Trio_%28Crabbe%2C_Malfoy_and_Goyle%29_1991b.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180607063603" decoding="async" width="245" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Trio (Crabbe, Malfoy and Goyle) 1991b.JPG" data-image-key="The_Trio_(Crabbe,_Malfoy_and_Goyle)_1991b.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2f/The_Trio_%28Crabbe%2C_Malfoy_and_Goyle%29_1991b.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180607063603" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Trio_(Crabbe,_Malfoy_and_Goyle)_1991b.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco attending a first year <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions class</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potions</a></b>: Draco was proficient in this area of magic. This could be because Snape favoured Draco and might have given him extra help in his class. Draco was able to pass his O.W.L. examination in the subject with a mark of at least '<a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a>' and most likely '<a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstanding</a>', since he was apparently not lacking a book or ingredients in Professor <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Slughorn</a>'s first class. When Professor Slughorn was teaching the subject,  Draco seemed to have lost his edge. He was covered in "something like <a href="/wiki/Cat" title="Cat">cat</a> sick" during a <a href="/wiki/Antidote_to_Common_Poisons" title="Antidote to Common Poisons">mixed antidote</a> composition, and producing a "merely passable" <a href="/wiki/Hiccoughing_Solution" title="Hiccoughing Solution">Hiccoughing Solution</a>. This of course could have been due to the immense stress and anxiety Draco was feeling throughout that year.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: Draco advanced to the N.E.W.T.-level class, meaning he achieved either an '<a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a>' or '<a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstanding</a>' mark on his O.W.L. exam.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He showed the ability to proficiently defend himself against dark magic.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">Non-verbal magic</a></b>: Draco mastered non-verbal spells before his sixth year, which included blocking <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinxes</a> non-verbally. This takes a lot of skill and concentration to do and only a few in his year have done it, given the high level of difficulty and precision required in the casting of spells this way.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/DracoQuidditch.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161221064226" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="326" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DracoQuidditch.jpg" data-image-key="DracoQuidditch.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/DracoQuidditch.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161221064226" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/DracoQuidditch.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161221064226" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/DracoQuidditch.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161221064226" decoding="async" width="180" height="326" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DracoQuidditch.jpg" data-image-key="DracoQuidditch.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/DracoQuidditch.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161221064226" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DracoQuidditch.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco in his Quidditch robes</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>He hadn’t been lying, he </i>could<i> fly well.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Harry admits Draco's talent in flying.<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">Flying</a></b>: He was quite a fine <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> player and <a href="/wiki/Broomstick" title="Broomstick">broomstick</a> flyer. He started flying at a younger age showing his skills in his first year. He made the team as a seeker in his second year, which was a very difficult position to acquire. Although his entrance into the team is enhanced due to his father bribing the team with the new <a href="/wiki/Nimbus_2001" title="Nimbus 2001">Nimbus 2001</a> <a href="/wiki/Broomstick" title="Broomstick">broomsticks</a>, he also had sufficient talent, although Harry still surpassed him in pure skill despite Draco's alleged experience and superior broomstick in their first game against each other. When Draco refused to play during his sixth year, his team suffered greatly due to the fact that his replacement did a poorer job, suggesting that no Slytherin during his time was more skilful than him.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/af/Skirmish_malfoy_manor.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141031142435" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="96" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Skirmish malfoy manor.gif" data-image-key="Skirmish_malfoy_manor.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/af/Skirmish_malfoy_manor.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141031142435" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/af/Skirmish_malfoy_manor.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141031142435" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/af/Skirmish_malfoy_manor.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141031142435" decoding="async" width="180" height="96" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Skirmish malfoy manor.gif" data-image-key="Skirmish_malfoy_manor.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/af/Skirmish_malfoy_manor.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141031142435" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Skirmish_malfoy_manor.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco duelling Harry and Ron during the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Everte_Statum.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402151706" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Everte Statum.gif" data-image-key="Everte_Statum.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Everte_Statum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190402151706" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Everte_Statum.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402151706" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Everte_Statum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190402151706" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Everte Statum.gif" data-image-key="Everte_Statum.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Everte_Statum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190402151706" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Everte_Statum.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco Malfoy duelling Harry Potter in 1992</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: Draco had been a very competent duellist for quite a while before starting Hogwarts, a skill probably inherited from <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">his parents</a>. He was able to cast the <a href="/wiki/Leg-Locker_Curse" title="Leg-Locker Curse">Leg-Locker Curse</a> in his first year, something <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> said no first year would be able to do. The very next year, he could cast such a powerful <i><a href="/wiki/Everte_Statum" title="Everte Statum">Everte Statum</a></i> that it threw <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">his opponent</a> across the room and even while subjected to a fit of laughter caused by the <a href="/wiki/Tickling_Charm" title="Tickling Charm">Tickling Charm</a>, was able to hit Harry with the <a href="/wiki/Dancing_Feet_Spell" title="Dancing Feet Spell">Dancing Feet Spell</a> accurately, the round ending in a standstill as a result. He later on was able to once again match Harry in their one-move duel, casting a spell as quickly as Harry did and causing their spells to ricochet everywhere. By his <a href="/wiki/Sixth_year" title="Sixth year">sixth year</a>, having been trained by Belatrix, Draco's duelling skills had improved to fare well against Harry, who had by the time faced much more experienced Death Eaters, delivering multiple spells nonverbally with ease and astonishing speed, something that most sixth years weren't able to do, and countering Harry's attacks, but Harry was ultimately able to cast <a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">a curse</a> quicker than him, exploiting the brief opening left by Draco when he was preparing to use Crucio to inflict what would have been mortal damage had he not been quickly treated. He was also beaten by <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> in his fifth year and by <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> in his seventh. At the age of forty, from what he himself admitted to having been years of practice, Draco's skills had greatly improved and despite his age he remained a very formidable duelist, capable of fighting Harry, who had been the Head of the Department of Magical Law Enforcement and Auror Office for several years by the time, to a draw, managing to land and dodge spells as much as his opponent managed to land on him, although Harry had not been fighting at full capability against Draco as he had no intentions to hurt or kill him but even Harry openly acknowledged his improved skills, and helping in overpowering <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a>.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Serpensortia.gif/revision/latest?cb=20200520234921" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Serpensortia.gif" data-image-key="Serpensortia.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Serpensortia.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200520234921" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Serpensortia.gif/revision/latest?cb=20200520234921" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Serpensortia.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200520234921" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Serpensortia.gif" data-image-key="Serpensortia.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d1/Serpensortia.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200520234921" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Serpensortia.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco casting the <a href="/wiki/Snake_Summons_Spell" title="Snake Summons Spell">Snake Summons Spell</a> in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Draco was shown to be talented in this field from a young age, as by his second year, he was already capable of <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">conjure</a> a <a href="/wiki/Snake" title="Snake">snake</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> which an advanced form of transfiguration learned in the sixth year and above, a reasonably impressive feat even if said conjuration is rather simple. He would also successfully qualify for the <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a>-level <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a>, meaning he achieved either an '<a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a>' or '<a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstanding</a>' mark on his O.W.L. exam.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> By <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">2020</a>, he easily used the <a href="/wiki/Incarcerous_Spell" title="Incarcerous Spell">Incarcerous Spell</a> when duelling with Harry and was capable of aiding Hermione, Ron and Ginny to successfully transfigure Harry into a doppelganger of Voldemort, displaying his high level of skill in the area, as <a href="/wiki/Human_Transfiguration" title="Human Transfiguration">Human Transfiguration</a> on the level of complete impersonation is a very demanding feat.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/POA_Draco_in_class_paper_bird_note.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190227202329" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="80" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="POA Draco in class paper bird note.gif" data-image-key="POA_Draco_in_class_paper_bird_note.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/POA_Draco_in_class_paper_bird_note.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190227202329" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/POA_Draco_in_class_paper_bird_note.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190227202329" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/POA_Draco_in_class_paper_bird_note.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190227202329" decoding="async" width="180" height="80" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="POA Draco in class paper bird note.gif" data-image-key="POA_Draco_in_class_paper_bird_note.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/POA_Draco_in_class_paper_bird_note.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190227202329" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:POA_Draco_in_class_paper_bird_note.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco making a paper plane fly</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Draco was talented in charms, as by his sixth year, he was able to cast the very difficult and advanced <a href="/wiki/Protean_Charm" title="Protean Charm">Protean Charm</a>, something that the only known student of the same age capable of was Hermione (albeit, he was known to have mastered it one year later than she could). In <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, he successfully disarmed <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a>. Draco was capable of casting a successful <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a> to block Harry Potter's spells in a duel. By his seventh year, he was able to cast the <a href="/wiki/Disillusionment_Charm" title="Disillusionment Charm">Disillusionment Charm</a> on himself to the point where Harry, Ron and Hermione could not see him and remain undetected, a highly advanced piece of <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a>. He was also capable of casting a <a href="/wiki/Paper_bird_charm" title="Paper bird charm">charm</a> which animates a paper bird to make it <a href="/wiki/Levitation" title="Levitation">fly</a> like a real <a href="/wiki/Bird" title="Bird">bird</a>. By <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">2020</a>, Draco displayed remarkable improvement in his skills in charm-work, making effective use of it in combat in his duel with Harry, notably able to rival Harry's <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a>, easily pushing a chair to block one of Harry's spells and later on stopping a chair flung at a high speed by Harry, along with being even able to use <a href="/wiki/Mobilicorpus" title="Mobilicorpus">Mobilicorpus</a> easily on Harry, making him bounce up and down on the table. Later on, he effortlessly used the <a href="/wiki/Levitation_Charm" title="Levitation Charm">Levitation Charm</a> to levitate Delphini out of the air and out of sight and proceeded to swiftly silence her with the <a href="/wiki/Silencing_Charm" title="Silencing Charm">Silencing Charm</a>.</li>
