<li><b><a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a></b>: Draco demonstrated a proficiency for dark magic from a young age, as he was quickly capable of casting numerous <a href="/wiki/Dark_charm" title="Dark charm">dark charms</a> to humiliate others during his Hogwarts years, such as the <a href="/wiki/Leg-Locker_Curse" title="Leg-Locker Curse">Leg-Locker Curse</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tongue-Tying_Curse" title="Tongue-Tying Curse">Tongue-Tying Curse</a>, <a href="/wiki/Knockback_Jinx" title="Knockback Jinx">Knockback Jinx</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dancing_Feet_Spell" title="Dancing Feet Spell">Dancing Feet Spell</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Hex" title="Hex">hex</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Densaugeo" title="Densaugeo">Densaugeo</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Melofors_Jinx" title="Melofors Jinx">Melofors Jinx</a>, <a href="/wiki/Trip_Jinx" title="Trip Jinx">Trip Jinx</a>, <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a> as well as an <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy%27s_unspecified_spell" title="Draco Malfoy&#39;s unspecified spell">unspecified dark charm</a>. In this <a href="/wiki/1996%E2%80%931997_school_year" title="1996–1997 school year">sixth year</a>, Draco learned how to successfully cast at least two of the <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curses</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a>, following his transformation into a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, allowing him to become a fully-fledged <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizard</a>. Both of these are extremely difficult and powerful dark <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curses</a> that not even many adult wizards can perform; his incredibly skilful Aunt Bellatrix might have taught him those while she was teaching him Occlumency and non-verbal spells. His Imperius Curse was strong enough to hold down <a href="/wiki/Rosmerta" title="Rosmerta">Madam Rosmerta</a> for almost an entire year, while he used the Cruciatus Curse to punish <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a>. It is possible he has the capability (but not the willingness) to perform the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a> as well. Whilst duelling Harry Potter in <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">2020</a>, he was able to swiftly and successfully perform a number of dark charms against him with ease, such as the <i><a href="/wiki/Levicorpus" title="Levicorpus">Levicorpus</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinx</a> along with Densaugeo and the Knockback Jinx, showing his skills in dark magic were still adept long after abandoning the Death Eaters. He even offered to be the one to disguise himself as Voldemort when he and the others went back in time to stop Delphini due to his knowledge and abilities in dark magic, suggesting he was assured he could engage in dark magic activities well enough to convince Delphini of his identity.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">Magical</a> repair</b>: Draco managed to repair the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts-Borgin_and_Burkes_Vanishing_Cabinet_pair" title="Hogwarts-Borgin and Burkes Vanishing Cabinet pair">Vanishing Cabinet</a> in his sixth year with some assistance from Borgin, though it did take him the majority of the year. The cabinet was smashed by Peeves in his second year and Draco repaired it despite the fact that the magical link between the two cabinets might have been damaged.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">Alchemy</a></b>: After graduating from Hogwarts, Draco began studying Alchemy as a hobby.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Possessions">Possessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Possessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Possessions"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 224px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Malfoy%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070114011607" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="222" height="35" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Malfoy&#39;s wand.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoy&#39;s_wand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Malfoy%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/222?cb=20070114011607" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Malfoy%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070114011607" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Malfoy%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/222?cb=20070114011607" decoding="async" width="222" height="35" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Malfoy&#39;s wand.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoy&#39;s_wand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Malfoy%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/222?cb=20070114011607" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Malfoy%27s_wand.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco's hawthorn <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy%27s_wand" title="Draco Malfoy&#39;s wand">wand</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy%27s_wand" title="Draco Malfoy&#39;s wand">Wand</a></b>: Draco's wand was 10" long, made of <a href="/wiki/Hawthorn" title="Hawthorn">hawthorn</a> <a href="/wiki/Wand_wood" title="Wand wood">wood</a>, and had a <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_hair" title="Unicorn hair">Unicorn hair</a> <a href="/wiki/Wand_core" title="Wand core">core</a>. The wand was manufactured by <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> and was described by him as being "<i>reasonably pliant</i>".</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Comet_260" title="Comet 260">Comet 260</a></b>: Draco owned this model of <a href="/wiki/Broomstick" title="Broomstick">broomstick</a> , which he owned prior to starting his first year.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Nimbus_2001" title="Nimbus 2001">Nimbus 2001</a></b>: Draco's father bought the entire <a href="/wiki/Slytherin_Quidditch_team" title="Slytherin Quidditch team">Slytherin Quidditch team</a> Nimbus 2001s in exchange for his son being played as <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a>.</li>
<li><b>Dress robes</b>: Draco wore dress robes while attending the Yule Ball with <a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a> in 1995.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy%27s_eagle_owl" title="Draco Malfoy&#39;s eagle owl">Eagle owl</a></b>: Draco owned an <a href="/wiki/Eagle_owl" title="Eagle owl">Eagle owl</a>, or <i>Bubo bubo</i>. During Malfoy's first year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Owl" title="Owl">owl</a> delivered daily packages of sweets from <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">his mother</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS9_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS9-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Prefect_badge" title="Prefect badge">Prefect badge</a></b>: Draco owned a Slytherin Prefect badge, which he gained after becoming a Prefect in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Potter_Stinks_badge" title="Potter Stinks badge">Potter Stinks badge</a></b>: Draco owned one these enchanted badges during the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, for the purpose of mocking <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Peruvian_Instant_Darkness_Powder" title="Peruvian Instant Darkness Powder">Peruvian Instant Darkness Powder</a></b>: Draco possessed some of this magical, darkness creating powder sold by <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes" title="Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes">Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes</a>, which he used in 1997 to smuggle Death Eaters into Hogwarts castle.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Hand_of_Glory" title="Hand of Glory">Hand of Glory</a></b>: Draco bought the Hand of Glory from <a href="/wiki/Borgin_and_Burkes" title="Borgin and Burkes">Borgin and Burkes</a> sometime after the end of his second year and before the start of his sixth, he used it to guide himself and the rest of the Death Eaters outside the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> after he used the Peruvian Instant Darkness Powder.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a></b>: Draco possessed a Time-Turner, passed down by his father. Unlike the Ministry-issued devices that were bound by a five-hour safety travel, this was a genuine device that allowed one to travel far back into the past. Also unlike the prototype possessed by <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Nott" title="Theodore Nott">Theodore Nott</a>, it was not limited by a duration stay of five minutes before returning to the present, as that one was produced with inexpensive metal. Draco kept the device as he thought of using it to see his late wife again, and Harry noted that keeping such a dangerous artefact could land him in Azkaban. Nevertheless, this Time-Turner was pivotal in saving the original timeline from <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a>'s interference.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Parents">Parents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Parents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Parents"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I haven't got any options! I've got to do it! He'll kill me! He'll kill my whole family!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> on Voldemort's threat to his family<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 177px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/DH-Promotional-Picture-draco-malfoy-27114107-960-1280.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130219114422" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="175" height="233" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH-Promotional-Picture-draco-malfoy-27114107-960-1280.jpg" data-image-key="DH-Promotional-Picture-draco-malfoy-27114107-960-1280.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/DH-Promotional-Picture-draco-malfoy-27114107-960-1280.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20130219114422" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/DH-Promotional-Picture-draco-malfoy-27114107-960-1280.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130219114422" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/DH-Promotional-Picture-draco-malfoy-27114107-960-1280.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20130219114422" decoding="async" width="175" height="233" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH-Promotional-Picture-draco-malfoy-27114107-960-1280.jpg" data-image-key="DH-Promotional-Picture-draco-malfoy-27114107-960-1280.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9b/DH-Promotional-Picture-draco-malfoy-27114107-960-1280.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20130219114422" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH-Promotional-Picture-draco-malfoy-27114107-960-1280.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucius and Draco in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius</a> and <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> both spoiled their only child. In <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, Narcissa sent packages of sweets daily to her son. In <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, Lucius bought broomsticks for the entire <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> <a href="/wiki/Slytherin_Quidditch_team" title="Slytherin Quidditch team">team</a> when Draco was made <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a>, and Narcissa often sent care packages to her son. She also refused to send Draco abroad to <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang Institute</a>, as Lucius originally wanted, insisting he stay closer to home by attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, despite Lucius's desire to keep Draco away from the influence of Muggle-borns in Hogwarts and also because Durmstrang Institute was known to teach dark arts rather than just the defences which was why Lucius Malfoy had wanted Draco a place in that school, but, finally fulfilling Narcissa's wish for him to study somewhere not too far from home.
</p><p>Lucius was colder and more demanding than his wife, criticising his son for getting lower school marks than <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> who was Muggle-born. Despite this, Draco greatly admired his father, often boasting about his influence and striving to be like him.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Also, as Draco attempted to use his grandfather's name, <a href="/wiki/Abraxas_Malfoy" title="Abraxas Malfoy">Abraxas</a>, to charm <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, Draco may have had a similar level of respect for his grandfather as for his parents.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 156px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/Narcissa_Malfoy_DH_promo_picture.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130810181232" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="154" height="232" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Narcissa Malfoy DH promo picture.jpg" data-image-key="Narcissa_Malfoy_DH_promo_picture.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/Narcissa_Malfoy_DH_promo_picture.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20130810181232" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/Narcissa_Malfoy_DH_promo_picture.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130810181232" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/Narcissa_Malfoy_DH_promo_picture.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20130810181232" decoding="async" width="154" height="232" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Narcissa Malfoy DH promo picture.jpg" data-image-key="Narcissa_Malfoy_DH_promo_picture.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/Narcissa_Malfoy_DH_promo_picture.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20130810181232" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Narcissa_Malfoy_DH_promo_picture.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a>, Draco's mother</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>It became clear during the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> that the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoys</a> cared about one another more than they cared for following <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>. Draco carried out the task he was assigned by Voldemort in his sixth year because his parents' lives were threatened, and appeared to be close to accepting <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>'s offer to keep them safe before <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> interceded to kill the Headmaster.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Lucius and Narcissa did not even attempt to fight, instead frantically searching for their son. Narcissa went so far as to lie directly to Voldemort about <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> being dead, in order to be allowed to return to Hogwarts and search for Draco, which also follows the saying that Harry Potter had been saved by a mother's love more than once.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Like his parents, Draco possesses the formidable skill of <a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">duelling</a>, <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curses</a> and is smart, quick and a smart retorter.
</p><p>However, after the war, Draco's relationship with his parents may have somewhat faltered, as his marriage with Astoria led them to think she is a somewhat disappointing daughter-in-law, mainly because Astoria's change of belief after the atrocities brought by Death Eaters' ideology, something they find unfitting for a fellow member of one of the <a href="/wiki/Sacred_Twenty-Eight" title="Sacred Twenty-Eight">Sacred Twenty-Eight</a> clans. Draco himself has lost his bigotry for less-than-pure wizards, and his willingness to let the Malfoy bloodline end at himself in order to preserve Astoria's health due to her blood-bourne curse earned Lucius' dislike. Regardless, he did not lose favour of his parents, as he inherited the Malfoy Manor and Lucius' collection of artefacts (which included the "true" <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> that proved instrumental later).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wife_and_son">Wife and son</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Wife and son">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Wife and son"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200621194235" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Malfoys on Platform Nine and Three-Quarters.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200621194235" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200621194235" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200621194235" decoding="async" width="220" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Malfoys on Platform Nine and Three-Quarters.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200621194235" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Malfoys_on_Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco with his <a href="/wiki/Astoria_Malfoy" title="Astoria Malfoy">wife</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">son</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sometime after the end of the war, Draco married <a href="/wiki/Astoria_Malfoy" title="Astoria Malfoy">Astoria Greengrass</a>, whose <a href="/wiki/Daphne_Greengrass" title="Daphne Greengrass">older sister</a> was in the same year as him at Hogwarts. They eventually had a son named <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius</a>.
</p><p>Draco and his wife evidently loved and cared for their son, raising him to be a better person than himself, proven when Scorpius has a crush on <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose Granger-Weasley</a> (daughter of Draco's former rivals) and is best friend of Albus Potter (youngest child of Draco's former arch-rival) he and his wife considered the day their son was born the best day of their lives. Astoria's death has caused Draco to be heartbroken, and he even considered using the illegal "true" <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> he received from his father as a means to see her again, though he barely resisted the urge. Draco would have gladly let the Malfoy family line end with him if it were to preserve Astoria's health, disregarding Lucius' wishes, but Astoria did want to leave behind someone for her husband, not for the sake of family beliefs. Draco certainly raised Scorpius more strictly than how Lucius and Narcissa raised him, as when Scorpius was to be punished by <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> for utilising the Time-Turner to corrupt reality to the point of reviving Voldemort, Draco stated he was prepared to listen to how his son is to be punished.<sup id="cite_ref-CC44_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC44-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bellatrix_Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Ah... Aunt Bellatrix has been teaching you Occlumency, I see.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 168px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140622235902" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="166" height="231" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange promo.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20140622235902" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140622235902" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20140622235902" decoding="async" width="166" height="231" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange promo.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20140622235902" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, his maternal aunt</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Bellatrix Lestrange was Draco's maternal aunt, sister of <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>. When Draco was younger he didn't have much contact with his aunt because she was imprisoned in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for torturing the <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> <a href="/wiki/Alice_Longbottom" title="Alice Longbottom">Alice</a> and <a href="/wiki/Frank_Longbottom" title="Frank Longbottom">Frank Longbottom</a>, who were the parents of Neville Longbottom, a fellow Gryffindor in Draco's year, into insanity. However, Draco did not feel any shame in his aunt's crimes against the wizarding world law that many would label as disgraceful. After Bellatrix escaped in Draco's fifth year at Hogwarts, she fought in a <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">battle</a> against <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and his friends and was the only Death Eater who wasn't captured; Draco's father, who had also fought, was imprisoned. After Draco was given a mission as a Death Eater, Bellatrix helped him and taught him <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>, nonverbal spells, and the Dark Arts. She also thought that Narcissa should be proud that her son became a Death Eater.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Bellatrix lived for some months at <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>, to be closer to Voldemort, who was also staying there. Bellatrix and Draco both participated in the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a>; Draco reluctantly watched Bellatrix's <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">torturing</a> of <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Bellatrix was killed by <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a>. 
</p><p>It is unknown how Draco reacted to her death, but it is likely he may have felt sadness as Bellatrix seemed to have some affection with Draco. However, given that Draco and his family regretted their allegiance with Voldemort, and that Draco abandoned his prejudice against non-pure bloods after the war, it is possible his opinion on Bellatrix changed considerably as she was fanatically loyal to, and obsessively in love with, Voldemort. Also, despite <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a> being Bellatrix's daughter, Draco did not hesitate to assist in her arrest after she had threatened his son's life.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_family_members">Other family members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Other family members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Other family members"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 164px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222048" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="162" height="216" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nymphadora Tonks DH promo headshot .jpg" data-image-key="Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/162?cb=20161119222048" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222048" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/162?cb=20161119222048" decoding="async" width="162" height="216" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nymphadora Tonks DH promo headshot .jpg" data-image-key="Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/162?cb=20161119222048" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, his maternal first cousin</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Draco was not close to his aunt <a href="/wiki/Andromeda_Tonks" title="Andromeda Tonks">Andromeda Tonks</a>, who had been disowned for marrying <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> <a href="/wiki/Edward_Tonks" title="Edward Tonks">Ted Tonks</a>, or their daughter, his cousin <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora</a>. Like much of the rest of his family, Draco likely held these relatives in contempt; Andromeda was considered a <a href="/wiki/Blood_traitor" title="Blood traitor">blood traitor</a> and Tonks was a <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a>. In addition, Tonks had married Remus Lupin, a werewolf, which the Death Eaters scorned to humiliate Draco. Since Draco was too scared of Voldemort to respond his feelings on the subject are unknown. Tonks refereed to him as "<i>The Malfoy boy</i>"  indicating she either did not know his name or despised him too much to care. Neither so much as mentioned their relation to one another. Similarly, Draco was indifferent to his first cousin once removed, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_17-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 163px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/14/Sirius-Black-Wallpaper-sirius-black-32913977-1024-768.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623160806" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="161" height="226" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sirius-Black-Wallpaper-sirius-black-32913977-1024-768.jpg" data-image-key="Sirius-Black-Wallpaper-sirius-black-32913977-1024-768.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/14/Sirius-Black-Wallpaper-sirius-black-32913977-1024-768.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/161?cb=20140623160806" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/14/Sirius-Black-Wallpaper-sirius-black-32913977-1024-768.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623160806" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/14/Sirius-Black-Wallpaper-sirius-black-32913977-1024-768.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/161?cb=20140623160806" decoding="async" width="161" height="226" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sirius-Black-Wallpaper-sirius-black-32913977-1024-768.jpg" data-image-key="Sirius-Black-Wallpaper-sirius-black-32913977-1024-768.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/14/Sirius-Black-Wallpaper-sirius-black-32913977-1024-768.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/161?cb=20140623160806" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sirius-Black-Wallpaper-sirius-black-32913977-1024-768.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, his maternal first cousin, once removed</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Both cousins were killed by Bellatrix, Sirius in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> and Tonks in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> respectively. His cousin, the illegitimate child of <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, his aunt, and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>, his former leader, was <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a>, whom he helped Harry Potter fight in the year <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">2020</a>, after discovering she was Voldemort's daughter, and after she tried to kill his son Scorpius. He did not have any love for Delphi, as he assisted arresting her for the murder of <a href="/wiki/Craig_Bowker_Junior" title="Craig Bowker Junior">Craig Bowker Jnr</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Vincent_Crabbe_and_Gregory_Goyle">Vincent Crabbe and Gregory Goyle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Vincent Crabbe and Gregory Goyle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Vincent Crabbe and Gregory Goyle"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Cursed Child"><b>Draco</b>: "<i>I always envied you and them, you know, Weasley and Granger. I had-</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny Weasley</b>: "<i>Crabbe and Goyle.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Draco</b>: "<i>Two lunks who wouldn’t know one end of a broomstick from another. You, the three of you, you shone, you know? You liked each other. You had fun. I envied you those friendships more than anything else”</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Draco admits the shallowness of his "friendship" with Crabbe and Goyle<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Cursed_Child" title="Harry Potter and the Cursed Child">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 249px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/POA_Draco_Malfoy%27s_gang.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170102053347" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="247" height="182" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="POA Draco Malfoy&#39;s gang.jpg" data-image-key="POA_Draco_Malfoy&#39;s_gang.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/POA_Draco_Malfoy%27s_gang.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/247?cb=20170102053347" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/POA_Draco_Malfoy%27s_gang.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170102053347" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/POA_Draco_Malfoy%27s_gang.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/247?cb=20170102053347" decoding="async" width="247" height="182" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="POA Draco Malfoy&#39;s gang.jpg" data-image-key="POA_Draco_Malfoy&#39;s_gang.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/POA_Draco_Malfoy%27s_gang.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/247?cb=20170102053347" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:POA_Draco_Malfoy%27s_gang.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco Malfoy and his cohorts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Draco’s two constant companions throughout his Hogwarts years were <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>. Crabbe and Goyle were often involved in Draco's confrontations with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and his friends. Though Draco often made it clear that he considered both of them rather stupid — a legitimate claim — and treated them more like lackeys than friends<sup id="cite_ref-POA_16-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>, he showed genuine concern for them and the rest of his <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">gang</a> on a few occasions; when Goyle was bitten by <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Scabbers</a> the Rat, Draco waited for Goyle before leaving, and he also showed concern for Goyle when he was hit by Harry's Curse, when Dumbledore expressed his disgust with Draco for allowing <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> "into the school where his friends live," Draco denied knowing he would be there, clearly disturbed by the sadistic <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a>'s unexpected presence. Draco's abrupt departure from his criminal activities left Crabbe and Goyle looking oddly lonely to Harry, as Harry was used to seeing Draco in between the two hulking boys, bossing them around.
</p><p>By the final confrontation between Draco and Harry in the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Draco no longer exerted much control over his friends; Crabbe, in particular, responded harshly to Draco's attempts to prevent them from killing Harry. Draco tried desperately to save both of his friends from the <a href="/wiki/Fiendfyre" title="Fiendfyre">cursed fire</a> Crabbe unleashed, helping pull Goyle onto Ron and Hermione's broom before letting Harry fly the two of them out, and was very upset by Crabbe's death. Although it was Ron and Hermione who saved Goyle from falling into the fire, if it wasn't for Draco who dragged Goyle to safety, Ron and Hermione would never had saved Goyle, so it can be considered that Draco saved Goyle's life.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">2020</a>, an adult Draco admitted to Harry and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">his wife</a> that his relationship with Crabbe and Goyle could never really have been called friendship, as they had little in common except the prejudices they had inherited from their families, and Crabbe and Goyle were far too stupid to be reliable cohorts in anything.  Draco also admitted that he had always envied Harry's close friendship with Ron and Hermione, in stark contrast to the emptiness of his relationship with his two "best friends" at Hogwarts.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pansy_Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Pansy Parkinson">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Pansy Parkinson"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Draco Malfoy</b>: "<i>I mean, I might not even be at Hogwarts next year, what’s it matter to me if some <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">fat old has-been</a> likes me or not?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Pansy Parkinson</b>: "<i>What do you mean, you might not be at Hogwarts next year?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Draco Malfoy</b>: "<i>Well, you never know. I might have — er — moved on to bigger and better things.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Pansy Parkinson</b>: "<i>Do you mean — <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Him</a>?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Draco telling Pansy about becoming a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 166px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Pansyinfobox.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110801070341" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="164" height="217" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pansyinfobox.jpg" data-image-key="Pansyinfobox.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Pansyinfobox.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20110801070341" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Pansyinfobox.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110801070341" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Pansyinfobox.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20110801070341" decoding="async" width="164" height="217" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pansyinfobox.jpg" data-image-key="Pansyinfobox.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Pansyinfobox.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20110801070341" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pansyinfobox.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a>, his friend whom had a crush on him</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Pansy Parkinson, a <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> girl in Draco's year, was a close friend of Draco's at Hogwarts. She often fawned over him, laughing loudly at his snide jokes, showing great concern when Draco was injured by <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a> in their third year,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_16-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> and accompanying him to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_3-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Draco and Pansy were both members of the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefects</a> in their fifth year,<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_17-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> which is indicative of their leadership roles in Slytherin House. They are noted as being particularly cosy in their sixth year at Hogwarts, seen in the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> with Draco's head in Pansy's lap, Pansy stroking Draco's hair, and wasted no time in vilifying Harry for (unintentionally) slashing Draco with <a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">a deadly curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Sometime after this period, however, Pansy and Draco's friendship waned. Whether she was ever his girlfriend is unknown, but Draco eventually married <a href="/wiki/Astoria_Malfoy" title="Astoria Malfoy">Astoria Greengrass</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Theodore_Nott">Theodore Nott</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Theodore Nott">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Theodore Nott"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Draco was also friends with <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Nott" title="Theodore Nott">Theodore Nott</a>, one of the few people whom he considered an equal, given that Theodore was just as <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blooded</a> and somewhat cleverer than him. However, Theodore was a solitary person who did not feel compelled to join any gang, including Draco's.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Theodore and Draco did laugh together at Hermione's blood-status once, and Nott was also seen with Draco and his gang after Harry listed their fathers names in a Quibbler article. It is also said that they had known each other prior to their arrival at Hogwarts.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Blaise_Zabini">Blaise Zabini</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Blaise Zabini">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Blaise Zabini"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>He was also friends with <a href="/wiki/Blaise_Zabini" title="Blaise Zabini">Blaise Zabini</a> during their sixth year, as they sat together at Hogwarts Express, where they discussed <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, who had all become members of the <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club" title="Slug Club">Slug Club</a>. Blaise was also one of the few people Draco had told about his mission, however he didn't seem to think highly of Draco's new position.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marcus_Flint">Marcus Flint</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Marcus Flint">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Marcus Flint"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Draco also appeared to be friendly with <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Flint" title="Marcus Flint">Marcus Flint</a>, as shown when Flint defended Draco against Fred and George Weasley, and again when he assisted Draco and his gang in their attempts to psych Harry out during a Quidditch game by disguising as dementors. Flint however did not hesitate to shout at Draco after he failed to catch a snitch despite it flying within his reach (he was too busy making fun of Harry to notice).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severus_Snape">Severus Snape</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Severus Snape">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Severus Snape"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Sir, why don't </i>you<i> apply for the Headmaster job?... </i>I'll<i> tell Father you're the best teacher here, sir </i>[...]'<b>"</b></span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco's opinion on Severus Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 166px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="164" height="232" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20081103135333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20081103135333" decoding="async" width="164" height="232" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20081103135333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, his favourite teacher and former head of house</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The teacher Draco initially respected the most was Severus Snape, <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> and <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Slytherin_House" title="Head of Slytherin House">Head of Slytherin House</a>. Snape, in turn, took Draco as his favourite student and showed him undeserved lenience on several occasions, which likely had something to do with Snape's long-time comradeship with Draco's father, or on the pretext of it, given that Snape defected from the Death Eaters. Draco even stated that Snape should apply for the position of Headmaster, after Dumbledore was suspended.
</p><p>However, after Lucius's imprisonment in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, Draco came to resent Snape, believing him to have usurped his father's place in the ranks of the Death Eaters, and that he was trying to take Draco's chance of glory as well. As such, Draco avoided Snape most of the year, refused any assistance, and even verbally assaulted him. However, Snape continued to protect him as when Draco was caught lurking outside of Professor Slughorn's Christmas party, and did not punish Draco when the boy refused to answer his summons to the office, something other students would not get off with so easily and which Draco took advantage of. Snape continued to protect Draco even after they fled from the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> together; when questioned by Voldemort about Draco's actions during his attempted murder of Dumbledore, Snape lied and told the Dark Lord that Malfoy hadn't lowered his wand and emphasised the young student's ability to get Death Eaters into Hogwarts as well as cornering Dumbledore, which allowed Snape to kill him. Snape's defence of Malfoy saved the boy's life and convinced Voldemort to free Lucius Malfoy from Azkaban, for which Draco reconciled with Snape.
</p><p>It is unknown how Draco reacted when he learned about Snape's death by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, or of his true loyalty to the Order of the Phoenix due to his love for the <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> mother of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>. However, given Draco's own disillusionment with the Death Eater cause and subsequent rapprochement with Harry, it is likely that Draco came to sympathise with his late teacher. In addition, it is possible that Draco's aforementioned detente with Harry as adults might have been motivated, at least in part, to avoid having a similar relationship that Snape had with <a href="/wiki/James_Potter" class="mw-redirect" title="James Potter">Harry's father</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">his friends</a> after their own Hogwarts years. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Bloomsbury Live Chat"><b>Interviewer</b>: "<i>Did Draco and Harry lose their animosity towards each other when Voldemort died?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>J.K. Rowling</b>: "<i>Not really. There would be a kind of rapprochement, in that Harry knows Draco hated being a Death Eater, and would not have killed Dumbledore; similarly, Draco would feel a grudging gratitude towards Harry for saving his life. Real friendship would be out of the question, though. Too much had happened prior to the final battle.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> regarding Harry and Draco's attitudes toward each other<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Bloomsbury_Live_Chat" title="Bloomsbury Live Chat">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 170px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="168" height="228" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/168?cb=20180528175859" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/168?cb=20180528175859" decoding="async" width="168" height="228" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/168?cb=20180528175859" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, his school rival and enemy turned ally and saviour</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Draco became Harry Potter's arch-rival almost immediately after they met, just before their first year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Draco was at first interested in Harry because he was so famous, but Harry was unimpressed by his arrogant manner. For the rest of their time at school, Harry and Draco loathed each other and tried one up each other whenever possible, although Harry compared to Ron was less prone to incorporating violence on Draco. This reached its pinnacle after <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> was sent to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> following the Battle of the Department of Mysteries.
</p><p>After finding out what Draco had gone through during their sixth year, Harry began to feel somewhat sorry for him, a feeling intensified by witnessing the use to which Lord Voldemort was putting him. During that year, Harry nearly killed Draco with one of the <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Half-Blood Prince's</a> curses (which he used by accident, unaware of what the effects of the spell were). Harry himself felt utterly horrified and guilty at what he did. However, despite their enmity towards each other, it should be noted that Draco showed great reluctance in identifying Harry and his friends when they were imprisoned in his home. In turn, Harry saved his life twice during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. It should be noted that the main reason behind Draco's enmity towards Harry was actually due to his jealousy of the latter.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Over the years, Draco and Harry made their peace as adults, but still were not friends by the time Scorpius and Albus started school. This later developed into a more cordial relationship due to Scorpius and Albus being best friends. Draco would grow to trust Harry's luck and instincts over the years, and knew that Harry was always in the thick of the action when it was necessary. Draco would grow to have a deep respect and friendly relationship with Albus Potter and trusted him with helping Scorpius heal from the grief of losing his mother. During the Delphini crisis, Draco would come to confess much to Harry, discussing at first in a rather distant manner, but upon revealing key details about his wife prior to and after her death as well as his family's hidden Time Turner, Draco and Harry finally came to a mutual respect for one another, and saw each other as friends for the first time, though it still did not heal everything from their marred past. Draco even admitted that he had always envied Harry, Ron, and Hermione's friendship.
</p><p>Draco is first cousins, twice removed, with at least <a href="/wiki/Charlus_Potter%27s_son" title="Charlus Potter&#39;s son">one member</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potter family</a>, through the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Black" title="House of Black">Black family</a>. Though it is unknown if he has any relation to Harry himself, of if they even know about that fact.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weasley_family">Weasley family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Weasley family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Weasley family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Think my name's funny, do you? No need to ask who </i>you<i> are. My father told me all the Weasleys have red hair, freckles, and more children than they can afford.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco to <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> when they first meet<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="146" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20200417054614" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20200417054614" decoding="async" width="251" height="146" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20200417054614" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_family.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Weasley family (excluding Bill and Charlie)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoy family</a> generally looked down upon the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a> for their lack of wealth and “<a href="/wiki/Blood_traitor" title="Blood traitor">blood traitor</a>” status, a sentiment Draco made clear immediately upon meeting <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> on the train to Hogwarts for their first year.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_15-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He and Ron had a hostility that mirrored that of their fathers, often insulting one another and prone even to physical fights at times. Draco also wrote the lyrics to the demeaning song <i><a href="/wiki/Weasley_is_Our_King" title="Weasley is Our King">Weasley is Our King</a></i>, which was meant to undermine Ron's abilities as a <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_17-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Crabbe set the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> on fire, Ron assisted Harry and Hermione in pulling Draco and Goyle away, but with some reluctance. When he and his friends saved Draco again later that day from a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> Draco was pleading with, Ron <a href="/wiki/Muggle_duelling" title="Muggle duelling">punched</a> him in the face and called him a “two-faced bastard”. Although this enmity seems to have faded with age, Ron discouraged his daughter <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> from becoming friends with Draco's son, <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Draco had less interaction with other members of the Weasley family. <a href="/wiki/Fred_and_George_Weasley" title="Fred and George Weasley">Fred and George Weasley</a> attempted twice to physically assault Draco; The first time was when he called <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> a "filthy little <a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>"<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> and the second time after Draco insulted <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">their mother</a> and <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">father</a>, as well as Harry Potter's mother, <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> (earning both twins, as well as Harry, a "lifetime Quidditch ban" from <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>) and made sure to hex Draco, along with other members of the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a>, when they left Hogwarts. <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> also had a few hostile encounters with Draco, most notably hitting him with a <a href="/wiki/Bat-Bogey_Hex" title="Bat-Bogey Hex">Bat-Bogey Hex</a> when the Inquisitorial Squad tried to hold her, Ron, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OTP_17-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OTP-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Draco also appeared to dislike <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a> and showed no respect towards him despite the latter being a prefect. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hermione_Granger">Hermione Granger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Draco</b>: "<i>Good, aren't they? But perhaps the Gryffindor team will be able to raise some gold and get new brooms, too. You could raffle off those Cleansweep 5's, I expect a museum would bid for them.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>At least no one on the Gryffindor team had to buy their way in. </i>They<i> got in on pure talent.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Draco</b>: "<i>No one asked your opinion, you filthy little Mudblood.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; after Draco becomes Slytherin <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a> and taunts the Gryffindor team<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 161px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/1Harry-Potter-Half-Blood-Prince-hermione-granger-19871338-299-399.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140625165714" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="159" height="233" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="1Harry-Potter-Half-Blood-Prince-hermione-granger-19871338-299-399.jpg" data-image-key="1Harry-Potter-Half-Blood-Prince-hermione-granger-19871338-299-399.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/1Harry-Potter-Half-Blood-Prince-hermione-granger-19871338-299-399.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20140625165714" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/1Harry-Potter-Half-Blood-Prince-hermione-granger-19871338-299-399.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140625165714" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/1Harry-Potter-Half-Blood-Prince-hermione-granger-19871338-299-399.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20140625165714" decoding="async" width="159" height="233" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="1Harry-Potter-Half-Blood-Prince-hermione-granger-19871338-299-399.jpg" data-image-key="1Harry-Potter-Half-Blood-Prince-hermione-granger-19871338-299-399.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/1Harry-Potter-Half-Blood-Prince-hermione-granger-19871338-299-399.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20140625165714" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:1Harry-Potter-Half-Blood-Prince-hermione-granger-19871338-299-399.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, his enemy and whom he used to bully</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Draco's relationship with Hermione Granger was coloured before the two even met, although they never actually interacted until their second year. Draco was raised to believe in the inferiority of <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a>, and by his second year, his father had told him he should be ashamed that Hermione beat him in all of his school marks. Thus, Draco often taunted Hermione, calling her the derogatory epithet "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>", but she refused to ever be bullied. During the period when <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Basilisk" title="Basilisk">Basilisk</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> was attacking Muggle-born students, Malfoy told his friends Crabbe and Goyle (really Harry and Ron using <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>) in the Slytherin <a href="/wiki/Common_room" title="Common room">common room</a> that he hoped Granger would be the next victim.<sup id="cite_ref-COS_13-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Although Hermione generally ignored Draco's taunts rather than getting into fights with him like Harry and Ron, occasionally the two would exchange sharp words and, in their third year, Hermione even slapped him for insulting <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_16-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> When he encountered the trio in <a href="/wiki/Madam_Malkin%27s_Robes_for_All_Occasions" title="Madam Malkin&#39;s Robes for All Occasions">Madam Malkin's</a> before the start of their sixth year, he asked who had given Hermione a black eye (the result of a <a href="/wiki/Boxing_telescope" title="Boxing telescope">boxing telescope</a>) so that he could "send them flowers".<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_18-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Despite his dislike for and prejudice towards Hermione, Draco still advised <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> to get her to safety during the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> riot at the <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_World_Cup" title="Quidditch World Cup">Quidditch World Cup</a> (albeit in a taunting manner)<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_3-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> and demonstrated reluctance to identify her to his aunt <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix</a>, avoiding even looking at her.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, when Ron encouraged their daughter not to associate with Draco's son, Hermione expressed a more conciliatory attitude.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_20-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Draco and Hermione became third cousins, once removed in law when Hermione married Ron Weasley. Draco's son Scorpius would eventually develop a deep crush and even fall in love with Hermione's daughter, Rose Granger-Weasley. Although their relationship slightly improved after the war, Draco quipped a few times during the ambush of Delphini in Godric's Hollow on October 31st, 1981, that he was both astounded and mildly enjoying taking battle commands from Hermione, finding the situation darkly amusing. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Neville_Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Longbottom, if brains were gold you'd be poorer than <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Weasley</a>, and that's saying something.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Malfoy opinion of Neville Longbottom<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
