<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Neville_HBP_1996.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220929" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="244" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville HBP 1996.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_HBP_1996.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Neville_HBP_1996.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220929" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Neville_HBP_1996.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220929" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Neville_HBP_1996.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220929" decoding="async" width="165" height="244" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville HBP 1996.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_HBP_1996.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Neville_HBP_1996.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220929" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_HBP_1996.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, whom he used to bully</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>The initially shy and clumsy <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville</a> regularly found himself on the receiving end of insults from Draco and his <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">gang</a>, and was often the butt of their jokes and pranks -- a fact which served only to make Neville clumsier and less confident. Encouraged by Hermione, Ron, and Harry to stand up for himself, Neville grew to be someone who was much more difficult to bully by his later years at Hogwarts, resisting not only the Slytherin students, but also <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto</a> and <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Neville proved to have made an impressive and complete turn around from his earlier years of crumbling under Draco's bullying, when he openly defied <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and beheaded <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, effectively destroying Voldemort's final Horcrux.
</p><p>Draco and Neville were fourth cousins, but both of them did not know about this relationship.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_staff">Hogwarts staff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Draco, Draco, you are not a killer.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Draco Malfoy</b>: "<i>How do you know? You don’t know what I’m capable of, you don’t know what I’ve done!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Draco and <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="224" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" decoding="async" width="165" height="224" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, his former headmaster</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> 
<p>Draco showed particular dislike for the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> Albus Dumbledore, who was in favour of complete acceptance of <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a>, a contradictory view to that of the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoys</a>'. As such, Draco often ridiculed Dumbledore's ideals and choices. He was excited at first when given the mission to kill Dumbledore, with the desire to redeem his family name and avenge his father, even daring to use the derogatory term "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>" in front of the Headmaster, the latter of which displeased Dumbledore. However, Dumbledore pitied Draco when he became a Death Eater, as he knew that Voldemort had forced Draco to his bidding by threatening Draco's parents. Furthermore, when Dumbledore offered to save Draco from the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, Draco seemed inclined to accept the offer before the exchange was interrupted by the arrival of his fellow Death Eaters. When Draco witnessed <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Snape</a> killing Dumbledore, he appeared horrified, which likely compounded his regret of ever becoming a Death Eater.
</p><p>Also before his fourth year, Draco referred to Dumbledore as a <a href="/wiki/Mudblood-lover" title="Mudblood-lover">Mudblood-lover</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_3-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 168px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127041001" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="166" height="219" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20101127041001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127041001" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20101127041001" decoding="async" width="166" height="219" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20101127041001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, his former <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">D.A.D.A.</a> professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Accustomed to the preferential treatment he received from <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, and reaping the benefits of his family's connections and status, Draco tried to use <a href="/wiki/Abraxas_Malfoy" title="Abraxas Malfoy">his grandfather</a>'s good name to get close to <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, though Slughorn did little more than ignore him. However, Dolores Umbridge, who was familiar with Draco's father, made Draco and his <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">friends</a> members of the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a>, and was quick to allow the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin_Quidditch_team" title="Slytherin Quidditch team">Slytherin Quidditch team</a> to re-form after she disbanded every other "Student Organisation, Society, Team, Group, or Club" with <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree_Number_Twenty-Four" title="Educational Decree Number Twenty-Four">Educational Decree Number Twenty-Four</a>.
</p><p>Draco showed contempt for the teachers who lacked status or didn't fit his or his family's standards of blood purity, such as <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, who was a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">Werewolf</a> and consequently tended to look ragged and poor; <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, an unkempt <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a>; and <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> (<a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch, Jnr</a> in <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">disguise</a>), who was an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> known for the extensive list of Death Eaters he had captured, as well as his intense paranoia. Draco refrained from being too openly contemptuous toward the ex-auror due to fear. Incidentally, during the Ministry's smear campaign against Dumbledore, the same three teachers were cited as "eccentric decisions" made by Dumbledore, and evidence of his diminishing competence in the position Headmaster. Draco often found himself at odds with <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Gryffindor_House" title="Head of Gryffindor House">Head of Gryffindor House</a> <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a>, who never played favourites with any student, least of all Malfoy, though he showed her some level of grudging respect, while she did not accept Harry's accusations of Draco's crimes without sufficient evidence. Draco similarly seemed to feel some respect toward <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>. Draco also disliked the caretaker <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a> because he was a <a href="/wiki/Squib" title="Squib">Squib</a> and never hesitated to punish Draco, although they did work together in the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Myrtle_Warren">Myrtle Warren</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=38" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Myrtle Warren">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Myrtle Warren"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>... tell me what's wrong... I can help you...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Moaning Myrtle trying to comfort Draco<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 168px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Myrtle_Warren_as_human.png/revision/latest?cb=20110809071526" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="166" height="211" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Myrtle Warren as human.png" data-image-key="Myrtle_Warren_as_human.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Myrtle_Warren_as_human.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20110809071526" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Myrtle_Warren_as_human.png/revision/latest?cb=20110809071526" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Myrtle_Warren_as_human.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20110809071526" decoding="async" width="166" height="211" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Myrtle Warren as human.png" data-image-key="Myrtle_Warren_as_human.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d6/Myrtle_Warren_as_human.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20110809071526" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Myrtle_Warren_as_human.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Myrtle Warren</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During Draco's second year, when the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> was opened a second time, Draco jeered to the <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">disguised</a> Harry and Ron that the first time the Chamber was opened, a <a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a> died — that "Mudblood" being Myrtle.
</p><p>During Draco's sixth year, when he was assigned by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> to kill Albus Dumbledore, he became stressed out from the difficulty of the mission and the consequences of failure. Surprisingly, despite Draco's prejudice against <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a>, Draco apparently visited Myrtle regularly in a bathroom, where he confided in and even openly cried in front of her. In turn, she was under the impression that Draco was a sensitive boy who was being bullied (which was true, though Myrtle would not have known Lord Voldemort was the one bullying him). This may be one of the rare moments that Draco showed something other than disgust for Muggle-borns, though it is unknown whether he was aware of Myrtle's blood status and connection to the Chamber of Secrets' opening during Voldemort's time at Hogwarts.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Voldemort">Lord Voldemort</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=39" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I haven't got any options! I've got to do it! He'll kill me! He'll kill my whole family!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco regarding Lord Voldemort and the mission he's been given<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Lord_Voldemort.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20080719185802" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="241" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lord Voldemort.JPG" data-image-key="Lord_Voldemort.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Lord_Voldemort.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20080719185802" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Lord_Voldemort.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20080719185802" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Lord_Voldemort.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20080719185802" decoding="async" width="160" height="241" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lord Voldemort.JPG" data-image-key="Lord_Voldemort.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Lord_Voldemort.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20080719185802" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lord_Voldemort.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, his former master and former idol</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Although Draco originally admired and respected Lord Voldemort, he came to fear him after having his family's safety threatened.
</p><p>Draco joined the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> at age sixteen, when <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> threatened to kill his parents if he failed in his mission to assassinate <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. In fact, Voldemort wanted to punish <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> for not retrieving a <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">Prophecy</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a> in his assumption that Draco would fail and have to be punished accordingly. Draco fought in several battles for Voldemort, including the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a>. After Voldemort's final defeat, Draco was not imprisoned, as he and his family had deserted the Death Eaters prior to Voldemort's defeat. 
</p><p>Although it is unknown if Draco ever learnt this, it was ironically his act in disarming Dumbledore before his death and unknowingly mastering the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> which prevented Voldemort from fully mastering the wand's power. Draco, in turn, was disarmed by Harry of his <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy%27s_wand" title="Draco Malfoy&#39;s wand">wand</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a>, thereby giving Harry mastery of the Elder Wand. When Harry told Voldemort these facts, the latter simply dismissed them, arguing that they made no difference and that Voldemort threatened to "attend to [i.e., kill]" Draco, likely as punishment not only for Draco's unintentional meddling but also for Draco's parents' disloyalty to Voldemort. Fortunately for the Mafloys, this arrogant indifference ultimately resulted in his final defeat at the hands of Harry Potter, 
</p><p>By <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">2020</a>, Draco had become so disillusioned from the Death Eater cause due to his experiences with Voldemort that he (Draco) helped the Trio defeat Voldemort's daughter <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a> in her plan to save Voldemort from <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_Godric%27s_Hollow_(1981)" title="Attack at Godric&#39;s Hollow (1981)">his first downfall</a> back in 1981. What was rather remarkable about Draco's involvement in this escapade was that Delphini was the illegitimate daughter of Draco's aunt Bellatrix, and therefore Draco's cousin. This defiance of Delphini and Voldemort demonstrated that Draco wanted so little to do with his erstwhile master that even having the Dark Lord's daughter being a blood relative was a repugnant notion to him. Draco also might have been motivated by a desire to redeem himself from his Death Eater past. During this period in his life, Draco also began referring to Voldemort by his name rather than the "Dark Lord" as he did in his youth, which might have been motivated by his self-redemption.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Slytherin_Quidditch_Team">Slytherin Quidditch Team</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=40" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Slytherin Quidditch Team">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Slytherin Quidditch Team"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Draco Malfoy was the <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> Team starting his second year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Malfoy appeared to be very popular with the team. This is most likely because during his second year his <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">father</a> bought the team new and faster brooms. Also, the rest of the team appeared to have the <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">same views</a> as he did because they smirked when Malfoy called <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> a "<a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Mudblood</a>" and laughed when a curse backfired on <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ronald Weasley</a> after the disagreement with Hermione Granger.
</p><p>Draco also appeared to be somehow related to one of the team members — <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Flint" title="Marcus Flint">Marcus Flint</a> — through <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">his maternal 2nd great-grandfather</a>, who married the <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blooded</a> <a href="/wiki/Ursula_Flint" title="Ursula Flint">Ursula</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Flint_family" title="Flint family">Flint family</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Media">Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=41" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Media"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=42" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 202px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/LuciusMalfoy1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20060702230550" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="200" height="239" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="LuciusMalfoy1.jpg" data-image-key="LuciusMalfoy1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/LuciusMalfoy1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20060702230550" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/LuciusMalfoy1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20060702230550" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/LuciusMalfoy1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20060702230550" decoding="async" width="200" height="239" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="LuciusMalfoy1.jpg" data-image-key="LuciusMalfoy1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/LuciusMalfoy1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20060702230550" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:LuciusMalfoy1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco's father and partial namesake, <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Draco's name, like those of many members of his maternal family, the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Black" title="House of Black">House of Black</a>, is derived from that of a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Draco_(constellation)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Draco (constellation)">constellation</a>. Draco is also known as the Dragon; <i>Draco</i> translates into "dragon" in Latin and "serpent" in Greek. The constellation is connected to multiple legends in Greek mythology, most notably as symbolising the hundred-headed dragon Hercules had to get past during his <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Labours_of_Hercules" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Labours of Hercules">Twelve Labours</a>, or the dragon killed by <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cadmus" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Cadmus">Cadmus</a> before he founded the city of Thebes. In Roman legend, Draco the dragon was killed by the goddess of wisdom, <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Minerva" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Minerva">Minerva</a>, and tossed into the sky. Another connection with him being a Death Eater, is the fact that Lucifer/Satan is referenced as a Dragon in Christian Theology. In addition, Draco was the name of an <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Draco_(lawgiver)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Draco (lawgiver)">Ancient Greek legislator</a> whose laws were notoriously harsh. The word <i>draconian</i>, meaning "unusually severe or cruel,"<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> is derived from his name. However, this Ancient Greek legislator simply wrote down laws that were already in existence. These harsh laws were already in existence in an oral tradition. He did not actively try to change these laws as they were written down for the benefit of the common people. This mirrors Draco's role as he introduces us to pure-blood mania, which is a philosophy he inherited from his family.</li>
<li>The name Lucius may come from the Roman dictator <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lucius_Cornelius_Sulla" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lucius Cornelius Sulla">Lucius Cornelius Sulla</a>, who extra judiciously executed his rivals. His name could also be a reference to the Roman Emperor Lucius Domitius Ahenobarbus, also known as <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nero" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nero">Nero</a>. Lucius is a name that derives from Latin meaning "bright" or "intelligent" and is related to the name Lucifer, the first name of Satan, which may reference Lucius Malfoy being bright but evil, or just evil.</li>
<li>His surname, Malfoy, in French (mal foi) means "<i>bad faith</i>."</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=43" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Draco_malfoy.png/revision/latest?cb=20200901014132" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="429" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco malfoy.png" data-image-key="Draco_malfoy.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Draco_malfoy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200901014132" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Draco_malfoy.png/revision/latest?cb=20200901014132" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Draco_malfoy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200901014132" decoding="async" width="180" height="429" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco malfoy.png" data-image-key="Draco_malfoy.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Draco_malfoy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200901014132" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_malfoy.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco Malfoy as seen in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Wizards_Unite" title="Harry Potter: Wizards Unite">Harry Potter: Wizards Unite</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Draco is technically part French seeing his ancestor Armand Malfoy was from France.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Technically, Draco was responsible for Harry missing two of his three Quidditch Cups at Hogwarts. In their fifth year, Harry was banned from the Quidditch Team by Umbridge for attacking Malfoy after he insulted Harry's mother and Ron's family. The second time, in their 6th year, Harry was forced to miss the final Quidditch match by Snape for using the Sectumsempra curse on Malfoy in their duel.</li>
<li>The first time Draco saw Voldemort was in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>, when the latter was sharing a body with <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Professor Quirrell</a>. Draco fled from him in horror, despite the fact that his father served Voldemort in the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. It is presumed Voldemort did not know who Draco was at the time, or if he remembered him when he became part of the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. Draco also probably didn't recognise Voldemort for who he was, since he was on the back of Quirrell's head, and that he was cloaked.</li>
<li>Draco would have attended <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang Institute</a>, a school that does not admit <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a> and teaches the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>, but his mother didn't want him staying so far away from home.</li>
<li>Ironically enough, it was Draco's wand that Harry used in his final duel with Voldemort, though it had changed its allegiance to Harry by that point. However, as it was the rebounding spell of the Elder Wand that killed Voldemort, Draco's wand did not vanquish Riddle.<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/df/TDHp2_Textless_Poster_Draco_close.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119213123" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="263" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="TDHp2 Textless Poster Draco close.jpg" data-image-key="TDHp2_Textless_Poster_Draco_close.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/df/TDHp2_Textless_Poster_Draco_close.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119213123" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/df/TDHp2_Textless_Poster_Draco_close.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119213123" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/df/TDHp2_Textless_Poster_Draco_close.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119213123" decoding="async" width="180" height="263" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="TDHp2 Textless Poster Draco close.jpg" data-image-key="TDHp2_Textless_Poster_Draco_close.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/df/TDHp2_Textless_Poster_Draco_close.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119213123" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:TDHp2_Textless_Poster_Draco_close.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Tom Felton as Draco Malfoy in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Screenshot_1142.png/revision/latest?cb=20150430175822" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="206" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Screenshot 1142.png" data-image-key="Screenshot_1142.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Screenshot_1142.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150430175822" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Screenshot_1142.png/revision/latest?cb=20150430175822" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Screenshot_1142.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150430175822" decoding="async" width="180" height="206" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Screenshot 1142.png" data-image-key="Screenshot_1142.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/48/Screenshot_1142.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150430175822" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Screenshot_1142.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco Malfoy as seen in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (video game)">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (video game)</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/Lego2_Draco.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100201172348" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="208" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lego2 Draco.jpg" data-image-key="Lego2_Draco.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/Lego2_Draco.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100201172348" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/Lego2_Draco.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100201172348" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/Lego2_Draco.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100201172348" decoding="async" width="180" height="208" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lego2 Draco.jpg" data-image-key="Lego2_Draco.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ed/Lego2_Draco.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100201172348" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lego2_Draco.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco Malfoy in <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_1-4" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Draco_LEGOD.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190517113714" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="248" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco LEGOD.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_LEGOD.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Draco_LEGOD.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190517113714" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Draco_LEGOD.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190517113714" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Draco_LEGOD.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190517113714" decoding="async" width="180" height="248" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco LEGOD.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_LEGOD.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fa/Draco_LEGOD.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190517113714" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_LEGOD.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco Malfoy in <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Dimensions" title="LEGO Dimensions">LEGO Dimensions</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Draco is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> actor <a href="/wiki/Tom_Felton" title="Tom Felton">Tom Felton</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)">film adaptations</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">Chamber of Secrets</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Goblet of Fire</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Half-Blood Prince</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Part 2</a></i> and so is one of the 14 characters to appear in all 8 film adaptations.
<ul><li>Tom provided the voice of Draco Malfoy in the video-game adaptations of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (video game)">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (video game)">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Draco is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> actor <a href="/wiki/Alex_Price" title="Alex Price">Alex Price</a> in the Original West End production of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Cursed_Child" title="Harry Potter and the Cursed Child">Harry Potter and the Cursed Child</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-mal_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mal-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a>'s early drafts of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, Draco's surname was "Spungen", "Spinks",<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> or "Smart".<sup id="cite_ref-PM_1-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Draco's wand is notable in that his wand is one of the few that have the same look throughout all eight films, though the prop in the last two films is all black instead of brown with a black handle.</li>
<li>Rowling has expressed some worry over fans of Draco: "People have been waxing lyrical [in letters] about Draco Malfoy, and I think that's the only time when it stopped amusing me and started almost worrying me. I'm trying to clearly distinguish between Tom Felton, who is a good-looking young boy, and Draco, who, whatever he looks like, is not a nice man. It's a romantic, but unhealthy..."<sup id="cite_ref-JKR_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKR-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets</a></i>, Draco does notice the Golden Snitch just after Harry does and chases after him for it only to get knocked off his broom and injured unlike the book where he never noticed it because he wasn't paying attention to his surroundings. Also for the film, Draco's injuries cause him to be sent to the Hospital Wing, though <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Madam Pomfrey</a> impatiently tells him that his injuries were not severe enough to be kept overnight.</li>
<li>In the the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, Draco's arm injury does not last as long as it does in the book.</li>
<li>It is shown that he is somewhat more respectful in the films than the books. In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire</a></i>, Draco is seen at <a href="/wiki/Memorial_feast_to_Cedric_Diggory" title="Memorial feast to Cedric Diggory">Cedric's memorial feast</a>. However, instead of talking and disrespecting the feast, he is seen looking down solemnly, mourning for Cedric.</li>
<li>In the films:
<ul><li>Draco seems to be less antagonistic towards Hagrid than in the books.</li>
<li>Draco seems to have a fondness for green apples, since he is seen eating one in <i>Prisoner of Azkaban</i> and putting one in the vanishing cabinet in <i>Half-Blood Prince</i>.</li></ul></li>
<li>In the film <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>:
<ul><li>Draco receives a hug from Voldemort and is the only known follower of his to receive this "honour". This scene was improvised by both actors, adding the "awkward" element.
<ul><li>This atmosphere actually makes sense, as Voldemort had never known love, and this act of hugging would seem strange to him.</li></ul></li>
<li>In the final climatic battle, he and his family depart from the battle and were not seen in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a> during the recovery from the battle.</li></ul></li>
<li>In the video game adaptation of <i>Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</i>, Draco appears to give his wand back to Harry to duel with Lord Voldemort. This was also filmed for the film, but it was cut.</li>
<li>He never referred to Ron or Hermione by their first names during the course of the original seven books. He did, however, refer to both of them by their first names by the events of The Cursed Child.</li></ul>
<h3><span id="Author's_comments"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Author.27s_comments">Author's comments</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?veaction=edit&amp;section=44" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Author&#039;s comments">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy?action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Author&#039;s comments"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Draco-Quidditch.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080929025219" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="213" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco-Quidditch.jpg" data-image-key="Draco-Quidditch.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Draco-Quidditch.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20080929025219" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Draco-Quidditch.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080929025219" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Draco-Quidditch.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20080929025219" decoding="async" width="160" height="213" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco-Quidditch.jpg" data-image-key="Draco-Quidditch.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Draco-Quidditch.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20080929025219" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco-Quidditch.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco Malfoy: Seeker</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;MuggleNet">"<i>He's shut down compassion — how else would you become a Death Eater? So he suppresses virtually all of the good side of himself. But then he's playing with the big boys, as the phrase has it, and suddenly, having talked the talk he's asked to walk it for the first time and it is absolutely terrifying. And I think that that is an accurate depiction of how some people fall into that kind of way of life and they realise what they're in for. I felt sorry for Draco. Well, I've always known this was coming for Draco, obviously, however nasty he was.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> regarding Draco's character<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/MuggleNet" title="MuggleNet">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> has commented that Draco is very capable of compartmentalising his life, which makes him skilled at <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> and at bullying others.<sup id="cite_ref-JKR_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKR-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>She also compared Draco to his first cousin once removed, <a href="/wiki/Regulus_Black" title="Regulus Black">Regulus Black</a>, in that they were both initially attracted to the Death Eater organisation, but "<i>the reality of what it meant was way too much to handle</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-JKR_34-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKR-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Rowling also compared Draco to <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley Dursley</a>; in addition to both being bullies, Draco was also "<i>raised as a pampered only son, indoctrinated with his parents' beliefs</i>". She has stated that there is "<i>a real moral cowardice to Draco</i>", but that he is not "wholly bad".<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
